<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="130d8fef83cc47a88c4b8cf6a64cf6c3"><span data-offset-key="130d8fef83cc47a88c4b8cf6a64cf6c3:0">A programming style which does not look at an object’s type to determine if it has the right interface; instead, the method or attribute is simply called or used (“If it looks like a duck and quacks like a duck, it must be a duck.”) By emphasizing interfaces rather than specific types, well-designed code improves its flexibility by allowing polymorphic substitution. Duck-typing avoids tests using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#type" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e17b772a5bd34d55a084d537e43713b7"><span data-offset-key="e17b772a5bd34d55a084d537e43713b7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">type()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f53d3ba61eec47129bd8c0cd9e3fe483"><span data-offset-key="f53d3ba61eec47129bd8c0cd9e3fe483:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#isinstance" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="38e8bcfed71d4bc7828267b378e6145f"><span data-offset-key="38e8bcfed71d4bc7828267b378e6145f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">isinstance()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d9f6ed94d4db46ca8583356baf834905"><span data-offset-key="d9f6ed94d4db46ca8583356baf834905:0">. (Note, however, that duck-typing can be complemented with </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-abstract-base-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0e41c644b0b54b0fb0c63a3225fc8e57"><span data-offset-key="0e41c644b0b54b0fb0c63a3225fc8e57:0">abstract base classes</span></span></a><span data-key="1c51597d1d9a481fac7d5a02e2f90da8"><span data-offset-key="1c51597d1d9a481fac7d5a02e2f90da8:0">.) Instead, it typically employs </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#hasattr" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a2e2f7afa4bd4e34a64669a73af15614"><span data-offset-key="a2e2f7afa4bd4e34a64669a73af15614:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">hasattr()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="33a52ebf4a1149d2962337a78fe6b0b2"><span data-offset-key="33a52ebf4a1149d2962337a78fe6b0b2:0"> tests or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-eafp" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="44a61739e025467ba39384aea97d5d4b"><span data-offset-key="44a61739e025467ba39384aea97d5d4b:0">EAFP</span></span></a><span data-key="f55c212e99b4427b896d18d6cc90a3b3"><span data-offset-key="f55c212e99b4427b896d18d6cc90a3b3:0"> programming.EAFP</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="38bb71fb099042d0b02f01074dd9fd33"><span data-offset-key="38bb71fb099042d0b02f01074dd9fd33:0">Easier to ask for forgiveness than permission. This common Python coding style assumes the existence of valid keys or attributes and catches exceptions if the assumption proves false. This clean and fast style is characterized by the presence of many </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#try" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7d42b2ed31c64261aed59db672012adf"><span data-offset-key="7d42b2ed31c64261aed59db672012adf:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">try</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2ec4ec5f10cc4fee8f656a6b257fae0a"><span data-offset-key="2ec4ec5f10cc4fee8f656a6b257fae0a:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#except" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="973450a6fc984afd9c66d634ba03b471"><span data-offset-key="973450a6fc984afd9c66d634ba03b471:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">except</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5a23f30b59b34d5093294eb595214dbb"><span data-offset-key="5a23f30b59b34d5093294eb595214dbb:0"> statements. The technique contrasts with the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-lbyl" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0f0fdb582a9747939cea751d3e257cb2"><span data-offset-key="0f0fdb582a9747939cea751d3e257cb2:0">LBYL</span></span></a><span data-key="a83fd768913a494187ab02d27cedcbfa"><span data-offset-key="a83fd768913a494187ab02d27cedcbfa:0"> style common to many other languages such as C.expression</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="237d8e95145247d88c0d8b6ff122ce15"><span data-offset-key="237d8e95145247d88c0d8b6ff122ce15:0">A piece of syntax which can be evaluated to some value. In other words, an expression is an accumulation of expression elements like literals, names, attribute access, operators or function calls which all return a value. In contrast to many other languages, not all language constructs are expressions. There are also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-statement" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b709785a860443cbba9711d9b977e669"><span data-offset-key="b709785a860443cbba9711d9b977e669:0">statement</span></span></a><span data-key="f8818a918de74d2e8258e25fbd6f7f09"><span data-offset-key="f8818a918de74d2e8258e25fbd6f7f09:0">s which cannot be used as expressions, such as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#while" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b7873dedc6fb40cdb4c142cc4023c390"><span data-offset-key="b7873dedc6fb40cdb4c142cc4023c390:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">while</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cb13f0e4d7ab4af48ae2acc211a3ee72"><span data-offset-key="cb13f0e4d7ab4af48ae2acc211a3ee72:0">. Assignments are also statements, not expressions.extension module</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="810284593d144cafb96f8876d9637c01"><span data-offset-key="810284593d144cafb96f8876d9637c01:0">A module written in C or C++, using Python’s C API to interact with the core and with user code.f-string</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ba707bbe502e4c419bc48d2b750d4da9"><span data-offset-key="ba707bbe502e4c419bc48d2b750d4da9:0">String literals prefixed with </span><span data-offset-key="ba707bbe502e4c419bc48d2b750d4da9:1">`'f'`</span><span data-offset-key="ba707bbe502e4c419bc48d2b750d4da9:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="ba707bbe502e4c419bc48d2b750d4da9:3">`'F'`</span><span data-offset-key="ba707bbe502e4c419bc48d2b750d4da9:4"> are commonly called “f-strings” which is short for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#f-strings" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="698e3a86a8a64c1fb3f446915057b982"><span data-offset-key="698e3a86a8a64c1fb3f446915057b982:0">formatted string literals</span></span></a><span data-key="8aafca88c62d4c3f90f8772fa65ba96b"><span data-offset-key="8aafca88c62d4c3f90f8772fa65ba96b:0">. See also </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0498" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ac8a6b202be942ab88f9229152b970ef"><span data-offset-key="ac8a6b202be942ab88f9229152b970ef:0"><strong>PEP 498</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="3cb4376978044740be1f615ccb036b70"><span data-offset-key="3cb4376978044740be1f615ccb036b70:0">.file object</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32"><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:0">An object exposing a file-oriented API (with methods such as </span><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:1">`read()`</span><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:3">`write()`</span><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:4">) to an underlying resource. Depending on the way it was created, a file object can mediate access to a real on-disk file or to another type of storage or communication device (for example standard input/output, in-memory buffers, sockets, pipes, etc.). File objects are also called </span><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:5">*file-like objects*</span><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:6"> or </span><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:7">*streams*</span><span data-offset-key="8583d48659ce4cbfb646a768d0da9d32:8">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2001cd63105b4bf19d4346b47fbbe481"><span data-offset-key="2001cd63105b4bf19d4346b47fbbe481:0">There are actually three categories of file objects: raw </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-binary-file" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4825bec8f1944c86a925d562c2e3a5c4"><span data-offset-key="4825bec8f1944c86a925d562c2e3a5c4:0">binary files</span></span></a><span data-key="bed6b639c17b4ad09f6c0943b2cdb477"><span data-offset-key="bed6b639c17b4ad09f6c0943b2cdb477:0">, buffered </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-binary-file" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="10af7806ac7a42fc8adb8758c5bcd799"><span data-offset-key="10af7806ac7a42fc8adb8758c5bcd799:0">binary files</span></span></a><span data-key="bd8a8cf5f8cc49cfa1f2096c6c6577bf"><span data-offset-key="bd8a8cf5f8cc49cfa1f2096c6c6577bf:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-text-file" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e4cc05fabebe473d9ddbf4583d33141b"><span data-offset-key="e4cc05fabebe473d9ddbf4583d33141b:0">text files</span></span></a><span data-key="f71708a36e8f467298e71e4c28695198"><span data-offset-key="f71708a36e8f467298e71e4c28695198:0">. Their interfaces are defined in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#module-io" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0aad7c5fd9d545de840a0d0dd5377046"><span data-offset-key="0aad7c5fd9d545de840a0d0dd5377046:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a29154fe45e240e6ab0fa7045b99b491"><span data-offset-key="a29154fe45e240e6ab0fa7045b99b491:0"> module. The canonical way to create a file object is by using the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="84c6feb168c3429c85aceb0bacac1139"><span data-offset-key="84c6feb168c3429c85aceb0bacac1139:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">open()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b24bb6b02ba2429e8efde5fc25a35259"><span data-offset-key="b24bb6b02ba2429e8efde5fc25a35259:0"> function.file-like object</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe41502170104f5e8db014fd061067d0"><span data-offset-key="fe41502170104f5e8db014fd061067d0:0">A synonym for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-file-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="393e0e6ca5164214ad8c5100df84a1ae"><span data-offset-key="393e0e6ca5164214ad8c5100df84a1ae:0">file object</span></span></a><span data-key="bff56fa7b79b4013a99a040ae0b85eb7"><span data-offset-key="bff56fa7b79b4013a99a040ae0b85eb7:0">.finder</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="840ac816413948c199ce74dd45d0930a"><span data-offset-key="840ac816413948c199ce74dd45d0930a:0">An object that tries to find the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-loader" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4754a1f684d749829fb1b67fd0fff905"><span data-offset-key="4754a1f684d749829fb1b67fd0fff905:0">loader</span></span></a><span data-key="0caa24bb22d24e5ea51ef3ff343386fb"><span data-offset-key="0caa24bb22d24e5ea51ef3ff343386fb:0"> for a module that is being imported.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dc57e42b56044ad887180d117ea69fa5"><span data-offset-key="dc57e42b56044ad887180d117ea69fa5:0">Since Python 3.3, there are two types of finder: </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-meta-path-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ab0b772b93a240c19d0b096c8076018b"><span data-offset-key="ab0b772b93a240c19d0b096c8076018b:0">meta path finders</span></span></a><span data-key="a7b1a129f84545ad92b8b9fe6727338b"><span data-offset-key="a7b1a129f84545ad92b8b9fe6727338b:0"> for use with </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a5dfc668af934201b1734770858223c3"><span data-offset-key="a5dfc668af934201b1734770858223c3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1e5b0c7a46b149dba5f0f303fc69206f"><span data-offset-key="1e5b0c7a46b149dba5f0f303fc69206f:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="72c0e9205cb74f3f800f4ee0c16bd085"><span data-offset-key="72c0e9205cb74f3f800f4ee0c16bd085:0">path entry finders</span></span></a><span data-key="f9422b7b60be46f298bec4ef5faf32bd"><span data-offset-key="f9422b7b60be46f298bec4ef5faf32bd:0"> for use with </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_hooks" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="340172f7d3ac470b9cecd4fa9cdd0316"><span data-offset-key="340172f7d3ac470b9cecd4fa9cdd0316:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_hooks</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3d15ad53b56746f08786586bbee5bc7d"><span data-offset-key="3d15ad53b56746f08786586bbee5bc7d:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b5614922710f43ac933775014236d081"><span data-offset-key="b5614922710f43ac933775014236d081:0">See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0302" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3fa90c7e09384287a62a85d4c5829e3e"><span data-offset-key="3fa90c7e09384287a62a85d4c5829e3e:0"><strong>PEP 302</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="5b41dd3b27ab42179a110b48ab259cd9"><span data-offset-key="5b41dd3b27ab42179a110b48ab259cd9:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0420" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="020777c1fbf64835a37688ef1518479a"><span data-offset-key="020777c1fbf64835a37688ef1518479a:0"><strong>PEP 420</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="81715529d59547abbfdbe29dc75201ae"><span data-offset-key="81715529d59547abbfdbe29dc75201ae:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0451" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ffd88c720c2f4f01ac4b9c2d07c9dbae"><span data-offset-key="ffd88c720c2f4f01ac4b9c2d07c9dbae:0"><strong>PEP 451</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="47d2817aaf8049cfa097313ca285abdf"><span data-offset-key="47d2817aaf8049cfa097313ca285abdf:0"> for much more detail.floor division</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec"><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:0">Mathematical division that rounds down to nearest integer. The floor division operator is </span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:1">`//`</span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:2">. For example, the expression </span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:3">`11 // 4`</span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:4"> evaluates to </span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:5">`2`</span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:6"> in contrast to the </span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:7">`2.75`</span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:8"> returned by float true division. Note that </span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:9">`(-11) // 4`</span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:10"> is </span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:11">`-3`</span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:12"> because that is </span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:13">`-2.75`</span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:14"> rounded </span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:15">*downward*</span><span data-offset-key="66f6e28e5ea643f3bdb64088e7a660ec:16">. See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0238" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e7f0a75c2f5d4c93822902dbaf956e7a"><span data-offset-key="e7f0a75c2f5d4c93822902dbaf956e7a:0"><strong>PEP 238</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="013f1db94e3a4ee0adb0d96396977ab8"><span data-offset-key="013f1db94e3a4ee0adb0d96396977ab8:0">.function</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8aa84c82f7b84b6ca2b46bdc7c766e83"><span data-offset-key="8aa84c82f7b84b6ca2b46bdc7c766e83:0">A series of statements which returns some value to a caller. It can also be passed zero or more </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-argument" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e3c5d32aec3747e3bcaf7a57600b852b"><span data-offset-key="e3c5d32aec3747e3bcaf7a57600b852b:0">arguments</span></span></a><span data-key="cea837fb708447039ddd2ec57ae5bb2d"><span data-offset-key="cea837fb708447039ddd2ec57ae5bb2d:0"> which may be used in the execution of the body. See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-parameter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dbfd492608234b4ebf7af2cf9dcf96e6"><span data-offset-key="dbfd492608234b4ebf7af2cf9dcf96e6:0">parameter</span></span></a><span data-key="26c3f39dc84a4e1595feadfaebbc731e"><span data-offset-key="26c3f39dc84a4e1595feadfaebbc731e:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-method" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c1e741a796ed45e081e87f2c45ed4b70"><span data-offset-key="c1e741a796ed45e081e87f2c45ed4b70:0">method</span></span></a><span data-key="713940c0508a4903b5d3d92bbdd961af"><span data-offset-key="713940c0508a4903b5d3d92bbdd961af:0">, and the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#function" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="66ed715af134476ca2e537402949ea50"><span data-offset-key="66ed715af134476ca2e537402949ea50:0">Function definitions</span></span></a><span data-key="36b64fa7eeec42e09bdec981248ff9f7"><span data-offset-key="36b64fa7eeec42e09bdec981248ff9f7:0"> section.function annotation</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="656df117af904e2280a8b070fb2303f0"><span data-offset-key="656df117af904e2280a8b070fb2303f0:0">An </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-annotation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0adbe9cea201467eb206f87eaf282bbe"><span data-offset-key="0adbe9cea201467eb206f87eaf282bbe:0">annotation</span></span></a><span data-key="f615272c55a64edd86b9f0364943a461"><span data-offset-key="f615272c55a64edd86b9f0364943a461:0"> of a function parameter or return value.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d5b64e751c004fb2b584cfcece7055b2"><span data-offset-key="d5b64e751c004fb2b584cfcece7055b2:0">Function annotations are usually used for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-type-hint" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="03c9cff41754446bb8faa229a66382b5"><span data-offset-key="03c9cff41754446bb8faa229a66382b5:0">type hints</span></span></a><span data-key="f5d27143a6094d09a66c795586670539"><span data-offset-key="f5d27143a6094d09a66c795586670539:0">: for example, this function is expected to take two </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c7bf419d4ce54d2bbbe06d87bb2b2443"><span data-offset-key="c7bf419d4ce54d2bbbe06d87bb2b2443:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="016dfc26b81142849af8f2da3c907d46"><span data-offset-key="016dfc26b81142849af8f2da3c907d46:0"> arguments and is also expected to have an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0f94b7f5f37241d4b3b552fb341f18f2"><span data-offset-key="0f94b7f5f37241d4b3b552fb341f18f2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d388dec65abc4c04945097f6950fd8ea"><span data-offset-key="d388dec65abc4c04945097f6950fd8ea:0"> return value:</span></span></span>

    def sum_two_numbers(a: int, b: int) -> int:   return a + b

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a2d4102849574646ad1a7bf4a3fa3d75"><span data-offset-key="a2d4102849574646ad1a7bf4a3fa3d75:0">Function annotation syntax is explained in section </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#function" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e385398b569c4136b6f8c640592482e7"><span data-offset-key="e385398b569c4136b6f8c640592482e7:0">Function definitions</span></span></a><span data-key="1e22cc0045de46e6800388d4e24eed79"><span data-offset-key="1e22cc0045de46e6800388d4e24eed79:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6e1de0e17464401ca91d23e782a752b8"><span data-offset-key="6e1de0e17464401ca91d23e782a752b8:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-variable-annotation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="78ccc6d815404bd8a4f9ee4b9976812b"><span data-offset-key="78ccc6d815404bd8a4f9ee4b9976812b:0">variable annotation</span></span></a><span data-key="a515758a24fe41b4a0970cde1bb47278"><span data-offset-key="a515758a24fe41b4a0970cde1bb47278:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0484" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ad5c93193bb7490bb187291c4709def0"><span data-offset-key="ad5c93193bb7490bb187291c4709def0:0"><strong>PEP 484</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="74c131b5bed24b45b46ce931582cc914"><span data-offset-key="74c131b5bed24b45b46ce931582cc914:0">, which describe this functionality.\_\_future\_\_</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c176ec51d761431ab4b43c73ae68d3ec"><span data-offset-key="c176ec51d761431ab4b43c73ae68d3ec:0">A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#future" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ce9b943ae2734d289cb3ef98064c7180"><span data-offset-key="ce9b943ae2734d289cb3ef98064c7180:0">future statement</span></span></a><span data-key="e871f53fe2794d9ca6b5b21af93d73ab"><span data-offset-key="e871f53fe2794d9ca6b5b21af93d73ab:0">, </span><span data-offset-key="e871f53fe2794d9ca6b5b21af93d73ab:1">`from __future__ import                                       <feature>`</span><span data-offset-key="e871f53fe2794d9ca6b5b21af93d73ab:2">, directs the compiler to compile the current module using syntax or semantics that will become standard in a future release of Python. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/__future__.html#module-__future__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8886899603d643409c1bce1607046dcd"><span data-offset-key="8886899603d643409c1bce1607046dcd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__future__</code></span></span></a><span data-key="3ca151b0385f4bbf9312030fb02b9a87"><span data-offset-key="3ca151b0385f4bbf9312030fb02b9a87:0"> module documents the possible values of </span><span data-offset-key="3ca151b0385f4bbf9312030fb02b9a87:1">*feature*</span><span data-offset-key="3ca151b0385f4bbf9312030fb02b9a87:2">. By importing this module and evaluating its variables, you can see when a new feature was first added to the language and when it will (or did) become the default:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> import __future__>>> __future__.division_Feature((2, 2, 0, 'alpha', 2), (3, 0, 0, 'alpha', 0), 8192)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1815e16f44d14921aa25457260a8f1a4"><span data-offset-key="1815e16f44d14921aa25457260a8f1a4:0">garbage collection</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b6563ee5c24046b39459a9fd33ef0715"><span data-offset-key="b6563ee5c24046b39459a9fd33ef0715:0">The process of freeing memory when it is not used anymore. Python performs garbage collection via reference counting and a cyclic garbage collector that is able to detect and break reference cycles. The garbage collector can be controlled using the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/gc.html#module-gc" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1e09b59c026f4448a9138aafeb0fe0b8"><span data-offset-key="1e09b59c026f4448a9138aafeb0fe0b8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">gc</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2479317902bc4f94a87d10ad9fb228fc"><span data-offset-key="2479317902bc4f94a87d10ad9fb228fc:0"> module.generator</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="33dd45f439e54544a77ff93dbcabf128"><span data-offset-key="33dd45f439e54544a77ff93dbcabf128:0">A function which returns a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-generator-iterator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7d0870e885bc45c1aa835987c7525697"><span data-offset-key="7d0870e885bc45c1aa835987c7525697:0">generator iterator</span></span></a><span data-key="764fc73de380480f946c4aaa31ced7cb"><span data-offset-key="764fc73de380480f946c4aaa31ced7cb:0">. It looks like a normal function except that it contains </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#yield" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d66dcb1ee1ee4c0b8bf03dfaf2a7a0b2"><span data-offset-key="d66dcb1ee1ee4c0b8bf03dfaf2a7a0b2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">yield</code></span></span></a><span data-key="23e8651579ba40609f4c18175cf51c32"><span data-offset-key="23e8651579ba40609f4c18175cf51c32:0"> expressions for producing a series of values usable in a for-loop or that can be retrieved one at a time with the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#next" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5a824f510122439c864cdc974fe8d786"><span data-offset-key="5a824f510122439c864cdc974fe8d786:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">next()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c041051d2bc5461faf25b76d9d490a07"><span data-offset-key="c041051d2bc5461faf25b76d9d490a07:0"> function.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5ff1cfb24ae54bb5b0614a87ca1274bf"><span data-offset-key="5ff1cfb24ae54bb5b0614a87ca1274bf:0">Usually refers to a generator function, but may refer to a </span><span data-offset-key="5ff1cfb24ae54bb5b0614a87ca1274bf:1">*generator iterator*</span><span data-offset-key="5ff1cfb24ae54bb5b0614a87ca1274bf:2"> in some contexts. In cases where the intended meaning isn’t clear, using the full terms avoids ambiguity.generator iterator</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c06e29c76d584697b3e31f323e90645b"><span data-offset-key="c06e29c76d584697b3e31f323e90645b:0">An object created by a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-generator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1fa57f6a8b9140bda40ba2bd580b4ea2"><span data-offset-key="1fa57f6a8b9140bda40ba2bd580b4ea2:0">generator</span></span></a><span data-key="accb3aa49e6b4104be47578b935c4d2f"><span data-offset-key="accb3aa49e6b4104be47578b935c4d2f:0"> function.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a9db8e5690964ff4aaf77960e5f3036e"><span data-offset-key="a9db8e5690964ff4aaf77960e5f3036e:0">Each </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#yield" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="938f639db9984637adbd91ba49624fef"><span data-offset-key="938f639db9984637adbd91ba49624fef:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">yield</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1a781e1650274651b1b02e01305dbaf2"><span data-offset-key="1a781e1650274651b1b02e01305dbaf2:0"> temporarily suspends processing, remembering the location execution state (including local variables and pending try-statements). When the </span><span data-offset-key="1a781e1650274651b1b02e01305dbaf2:1">*generator iterator*</span><span data-offset-key="1a781e1650274651b1b02e01305dbaf2:2"> resumes, it picks up where it left off (in contrast to functions which start fresh on every invocation).generator expression</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="314dcda022554588bb157ec432b2a4b4"><span data-offset-key="314dcda022554588bb157ec432b2a4b4:0">An expression that returns an iterator. It looks like a normal expression followed by a </span><span data-offset-key="314dcda022554588bb157ec432b2a4b4:1">`for`</span><span data-offset-key="314dcda022554588bb157ec432b2a4b4:2"> clause defining a loop variable, range, and an optional </span><span data-offset-key="314dcda022554588bb157ec432b2a4b4:3">`if`</span><span data-offset-key="314dcda022554588bb157ec432b2a4b4:4"> clause. The combined expression generates values for an enclosing function:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> sum(i*i for i in range(10))         # sum of squares 0, 1, 4, ... 81285

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f97ecdd66528420f8174af379eda97bf"><span data-offset-key="f97ecdd66528420f8174af379eda97bf:0">generic function</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0d1d038b34034cd59946a6980d436315"><span data-offset-key="0d1d038b34034cd59946a6980d436315:0">A function composed of multiple functions implementing the same operation for different types. Which implementation should be used during a call is determined by the dispatch algorithm.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6e1655dcb8714205b5fea22fe4af436f"><span data-offset-key="6e1655dcb8714205b5fea22fe4af436f:0">See also the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-single-dispatch" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ecd32cff228e44439e897877aff2ccc6"><span data-offset-key="ecd32cff228e44439e897877aff2ccc6:0">single dispatch</span></span></a><span data-key="5428636e4a184f8e9cbe2d5ee8751f16"><span data-offset-key="5428636e4a184f8e9cbe2d5ee8751f16:0"> glossary entry, the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functools.html#functools.singledispatch" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="db114d81ff184d27b58b590dc456d2ff"><span data-offset-key="db114d81ff184d27b58b590dc456d2ff:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">functools.singledispatch()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="84270da5d4da44f3ab3e20887d11b96d"><span data-offset-key="84270da5d4da44f3ab3e20887d11b96d:0"> decorator, and </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0443" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6b4905a2f62f459f9987cf1930c80952"><span data-offset-key="6b4905a2f62f459f9987cf1930c80952:0"><strong>PEP 443</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="82849bf68925439e84d06fe76bde22c3"><span data-offset-key="82849bf68925439e84d06fe76bde22c3:0">.generic type</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8850c24a7ae3435bb9b67698e2046d52"><span data-offset-key="8850c24a7ae3435bb9b67698e2046d52:0">A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-type" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="33c1a1a3325147f8953ed0744b9f2ab8"><span data-offset-key="33c1a1a3325147f8953ed0744b9f2ab8:0">type</span></span></a><span data-key="dd5fcbe6b3b9490398b546de0b73c9d5"><span data-offset-key="dd5fcbe6b3b9490398b546de0b73c9d5:0"> that can be parameterized; typically a container like </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="79c73d3907a346cf991971a19b77b222"><span data-offset-key="79c73d3907a346cf991971a19b77b222:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cc63969c009245cca6a7b574f9621cee"><span data-offset-key="cc63969c009245cca6a7b574f9621cee:0">. Used for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-type-hint" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fb929446ddb846f4aae6abd64a3d7cb0"><span data-offset-key="fb929446ddb846f4aae6abd64a3d7cb0:0">type hints</span></span></a><span data-key="6340b0e40c6f4dc4b11de6c3fde911a0"><span data-offset-key="6340b0e40c6f4dc4b11de6c3fde911a0:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-annotation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c8a30a292a424dca8cf82c9260636f3b"><span data-offset-key="c8a30a292a424dca8cf82c9260636f3b:0">annotations</span></span></a><span data-key="8d6985ee052641c084910accd8d7b29f"><span data-offset-key="8d6985ee052641c084910accd8d7b29f:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d85530de069744e6bf5831a6fb9028c6"><span data-offset-key="d85530de069744e6bf5831a6fb9028c6:0">See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0483" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9893f4f426ea4b3590e809add94dfe5f"><span data-offset-key="9893f4f426ea4b3590e809add94dfe5f:0"><strong>PEP 483</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="0c5a1e3e54814f42b9e6fedbc0310393"><span data-offset-key="0c5a1e3e54814f42b9e6fedbc0310393:0"> for more details, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/typing.html#module-typing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a1ff490c79d145bead0131889c72341e"><span data-offset-key="a1ff490c79d145bead0131889c72341e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">typing</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f6e345db05a243f8884de7e60433ad63"><span data-offset-key="f6e345db05a243f8884de7e60433ad63:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#types-genericalias" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f948865a8eae4e7d8a2114476c3ca010"><span data-offset-key="f948865a8eae4e7d8a2114476c3ca010:0">generic alias type</span></span></a><span data-key="635f14a408f6479ea714a6040de37867"><span data-offset-key="635f14a408f6479ea714a6040de37867:0"> for its uses.GIL</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e41f11fbfda24d3b945d058077f9ae6d"><span data-offset-key="e41f11fbfda24d3b945d058077f9ae6d:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-global-interpreter-lock" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a4faad7e30264451a37f06fa183e89ec"><span data-offset-key="a4faad7e30264451a37f06fa183e89ec:0">global interpreter lock</span></span></a><span data-key="f699eca4298b43ceb8cb737b23245ea5"><span data-offset-key="f699eca4298b43ceb8cb737b23245ea5:0">.global interpreter lock</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b966329ce524d9184bf9b9f7c9a48f9"><span data-offset-key="1b966329ce524d9184bf9b9f7c9a48f9:0">The mechanism used by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-cpython" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fab2f2111ad2445898f8cbf512e6206b"><span data-offset-key="fab2f2111ad2445898f8cbf512e6206b:0">CPython</span></span></a><span data-key="6571fe86ef5941fe92eb79504d9bbfd5"><span data-offset-key="6571fe86ef5941fe92eb79504d9bbfd5:0"> interpreter to assure that only one thread executes Python </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytecode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="744d3923c37142bebcdd05d5c8c4b49e"><span data-offset-key="744d3923c37142bebcdd05d5c8c4b49e:0">bytecode</span></span></a><span data-key="cf1a4f67e33e46cca2c13e0f8b776ce5"><span data-offset-key="cf1a4f67e33e46cca2c13e0f8b776ce5:0"> at a time. This simplifies the CPython implementation by making the object model (including critical built-in types such as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dffdf56fc3584bd2a9abea9410449122"><span data-offset-key="dffdf56fc3584bd2a9abea9410449122:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e4162dc14f3342f18c333cb6aa1aa1ab"><span data-offset-key="e4162dc14f3342f18c333cb6aa1aa1ab:0">) implicitly safe against concurrent access. Locking the entire interpreter makes it easier for the interpreter to be multi-threaded, at the expense of much of the parallelism afforded by multi-processor machines.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7aa6d07f4a61417489bc5550f5ef9e0f"><span data-offset-key="7aa6d07f4a61417489bc5550f5ef9e0f:0">However, some extension modules, either standard or third-party, are designed so as to release the GIL when doing computationally-intensive tasks such as compression or hashing. Also, the GIL is always released when doing I/O.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b3c65f9d0928444babc2018b32519a4f"><span data-offset-key="b3c65f9d0928444babc2018b32519a4f:0">Past efforts to create a “free-threaded” interpreter (one which locks shared data at a much finer granularity) have not been successful because performance suffered in the common single-processor case. It is believed that overcoming this performance issue would make the implementation much more complicated and therefore costlier to maintain.hash-based pyc</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2b9de87e05004db79286aff8ccd20071"><span data-offset-key="2b9de87e05004db79286aff8ccd20071:0">A bytecode cache file that uses the hash rather than the last-modified time of the corresponding source file to determine its validity. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/import.html#pyc-invalidation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b4054a12ccf4475fb81eab6f65547b2f"><span data-offset-key="b4054a12ccf4475fb81eab6f65547b2f:0">Cached bytecode invalidation</span></span></a><span data-key="3334c83b083a46648e912ad17a48bbc3"><span data-offset-key="3334c83b083a46648e912ad17a48bbc3:0">.hashable</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b22de25122c4e2ea5e154a3615f7181"><span data-offset-key="1b22de25122c4e2ea5e154a3615f7181:0">An object is </span><span data-offset-key="1b22de25122c4e2ea5e154a3615f7181:1">*hashable*</span><span data-offset-key="1b22de25122c4e2ea5e154a3615f7181:2"> if it has a hash value which never changes during its lifetime (it needs a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__hash__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="61f339ce14f947d2baf6d8318ee44ed9"><span data-offset-key="61f339ce14f947d2baf6d8318ee44ed9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__hash__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8e4d68c24e08406a82d2e3bfb239f6a9"><span data-offset-key="8e4d68c24e08406a82d2e3bfb239f6a9:0"> method), and can be compared to other objects (it needs an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__eq__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f80a8e9a56ce4a26b3d0c1ba59753881"><span data-offset-key="f80a8e9a56ce4a26b3d0c1ba59753881:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__eq__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f6ff0c7713554e84bf765399744f11c9"><span data-offset-key="f6ff0c7713554e84bf765399744f11c9:0"> method). Hashable objects which compare equal must have the same hash value.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b06955d4feda41e28a78bc0214858163"><span data-offset-key="b06955d4feda41e28a78bc0214858163:0">Hashability makes an object usable as a dictionary key and a set member, because these data structures use the hash value internally.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d25e578e5ec74687b83f5d7668da40d8"><span data-offset-key="d25e578e5ec74687b83f5d7668da40d8:0">Most of Python’s immutable built-in objects are hashable; mutable containers (such as lists or dictionaries) are not; immutable containers (such as tuples and frozensets) are only hashable if their elements are hashable. Objects which are instances of user-defined classes are hashable by default. They all compare unequal (except with themselves), and their hash value is derived from their </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#id" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="26e851bb45a8479090a264187257108d"><span data-offset-key="26e851bb45a8479090a264187257108d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">id()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="32d69158a82a40088ba962d710bf76e1"><span data-offset-key="32d69158a82a40088ba962d710bf76e1:0">.IDLE</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="be541703e1474cc592a4981884362b21"><span data-offset-key="be541703e1474cc592a4981884362b21:0">An Integrated Development Environment for Python. IDLE is a basic editor and interpreter environment which ships with the standard distribution of Python.immutable</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="165df418fa7a4585843429222781699a"><span data-offset-key="165df418fa7a4585843429222781699a:0">An object with a fixed value. Immutable objects include numbers, strings and tuples. Such an object cannot be altered. A new object has to be created if a different value has to be stored. They play an important role in places where a constant hash value is needed, for example as a key in a dictionary.import path</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="04b3420b195846a79840937d5f2fb269"><span data-offset-key="04b3420b195846a79840937d5f2fb269:0">A list of locations (or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="14fa447a27304e1fbfd653b5f89c2e0a"><span data-offset-key="14fa447a27304e1fbfd653b5f89c2e0a:0">path entries</span></span></a><span data-key="a6e9513bef4f44a1a5417efce1879ade"><span data-offset-key="a6e9513bef4f44a1a5417efce1879ade:0">) that are searched by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-based-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3cc576a023be4ea6a1c4973d501609ae"><span data-offset-key="3cc576a023be4ea6a1c4973d501609ae:0">path based finder</span></span></a><span data-key="285bcb7dc8104c929c985c8d68bfba5e"><span data-offset-key="285bcb7dc8104c929c985c8d68bfba5e:0"> for modules to import. During import, this list of locations usually comes from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1cb5af6dd40e4046876cae16047dc137"><span data-offset-key="1cb5af6dd40e4046876cae16047dc137:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="52547a272bf247a99dfba572b5a5977d"><span data-offset-key="52547a272bf247a99dfba572b5a5977d:0">, but for subpackages it may also come from the parent package’s </span><span data-offset-key="52547a272bf247a99dfba572b5a5977d:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="52547a272bf247a99dfba572b5a5977d:2"> attribute.importing</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a92cfa6fa6194121b85c0cc92631062d"><span data-offset-key="a92cfa6fa6194121b85c0cc92631062d:0">The process by which Python code in one module is made available to Python code in another module.importer</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b0a7ad108cc5430d8e6a3f15ad3de0a2"><span data-offset-key="b0a7ad108cc5430d8e6a3f15ad3de0a2:0">An object that both finds and loads a module; both a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c0fc5add2c0d4209a25d30d0c3370a49"><span data-offset-key="c0fc5add2c0d4209a25d30d0c3370a49:0">finder</span></span></a><span data-key="eea786233cf8462baad67cf54c2e71b2"><span data-offset-key="eea786233cf8462baad67cf54c2e71b2:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-loader" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2feeb92aa09d4ffa937bf4416cd3f9e5"><span data-offset-key="2feeb92aa09d4ffa937bf4416cd3f9e5:0">loader</span></span></a><span data-key="f1b80027ac5744c4bfa37e1871181ea5"><span data-offset-key="f1b80027ac5744c4bfa37e1871181ea5:0"> object.interactive</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="793fff2dcd5140c28a977af8a19862d1"><span data-offset-key="793fff2dcd5140c28a977af8a19862d1:0">Python has an interactive interpreter which means you can enter statements and expressions at the interpreter prompt, immediately execute them and see their results. Just launch </span><span data-offset-key="793fff2dcd5140c28a977af8a19862d1:1">`python`</span><span data-offset-key="793fff2dcd5140c28a977af8a19862d1:2"> with no arguments (possibly by selecting it from your computer’s main menu). It is a very powerful way to test out new ideas or inspect modules and packages (remember </span><span data-offset-key="793fff2dcd5140c28a977af8a19862d1:3">`help(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="793fff2dcd5140c28a977af8a19862d1:4">).interpreted</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="668afcadd5424f02af74298fda2c0526"><span data-offset-key="668afcadd5424f02af74298fda2c0526:0">Python is an interpreted language, as opposed to a compiled one, though the distinction can be blurry because of the presence of the bytecode compiler. This means that source files can be run directly without explicitly creating an executable which is then run. Interpreted languages typically have a shorter development/debug cycle than compiled ones, though their programs generally also run more slowly. See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-interactive" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c775c40bae4d4785ba01cb89a054237c"><span data-offset-key="c775c40bae4d4785ba01cb89a054237c:0">interactive</span></span></a><span data-key="016d45ec33fd4116b63a530decfb287c"><span data-offset-key="016d45ec33fd4116b63a530decfb287c:0">.interpreter shutdown</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1f9bf8c7f1d04e7ea7a7066e69514537"><span data-offset-key="1f9bf8c7f1d04e7ea7a7066e69514537:0">When asked to shut down, the Python interpreter enters a special phase where it gradually releases all allocated resources, such as modules and various critical internal structures. It also makes several calls to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-garbage-collection" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2e8b463f874f4cb5a9047237992f41f6"><span data-offset-key="2e8b463f874f4cb5a9047237992f41f6:0">garbage collector</span></span></a><span data-key="89b3f4fc93054628a0acc79b87f0efac"><span data-offset-key="89b3f4fc93054628a0acc79b87f0efac:0">. This can trigger the execution of code in user-defined destructors or weakref callbacks. Code executed during the shutdown phase can encounter various exceptions as the resources it relies on may not function anymore (common examples are library modules or the warnings machinery).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="95f3212ee0254a38a410eca98a59e3a8"><span data-offset-key="95f3212ee0254a38a410eca98a59e3a8:0">The main reason for interpreter shutdown is that the </span><span data-offset-key="95f3212ee0254a38a410eca98a59e3a8:1">`__main__`</span><span data-offset-key="95f3212ee0254a38a410eca98a59e3a8:2"> module or the script being run has finished executing.iterable</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fb7776b0f9734cb8b6c0d1b9e34ed46e"><span data-offset-key="fb7776b0f9734cb8b6c0d1b9e34ed46e:0">An object capable of returning its members one at a time. Examples of iterables include all sequence types (such as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="229296b650f54f0dbcba704471ebe070"><span data-offset-key="229296b650f54f0dbcba704471ebe070:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="08547c6e28fb41d58775cf5d9ec28920"><span data-offset-key="08547c6e28fb41d58775cf5d9ec28920:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8b39d81f3de14538bd1a7d3de4099056"><span data-offset-key="8b39d81f3de14538bd1a7d3de4099056:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2c6a2b5a1e9447859211820bc3951031"><span data-offset-key="2c6a2b5a1e9447859211820bc3951031:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f705e81ad81e43abad707aae8b29fb08"><span data-offset-key="f705e81ad81e43abad707aae8b29fb08:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tuple</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a2cb25c24bcc45339ea5f93616e9de5f"><span data-offset-key="a2cb25c24bcc45339ea5f93616e9de5f:0">) and some non-sequence types like </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1a8738f7d92240aca77234cc25c7f244"><span data-offset-key="1a8738f7d92240aca77234cc25c7f244:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="80740c231488463185084830089dd5c9"><span data-offset-key="80740c231488463185084830089dd5c9:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-file-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="72b255b0c5e34be58e993a005d10155d"><span data-offset-key="72b255b0c5e34be58e993a005d10155d:0">file objects</span></span></a><span data-key="422c33e039c3472bbb30b2e565798d8c"><span data-offset-key="422c33e039c3472bbb30b2e565798d8c:0">, and objects of any classes you define with an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__iter__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1347bdf91c81486caa14b082191e38b2"><span data-offset-key="1347bdf91c81486caa14b082191e38b2:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__iter__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="533018cd8bfb4a399aaac48937a41b76"><span data-offset-key="533018cd8bfb4a399aaac48937a41b76:0"> method or with a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f2d4c24ddcb94614ba09007eb1e5fd6c"><span data-offset-key="f2d4c24ddcb94614ba09007eb1e5fd6c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="72fc266117cd40f7a90f20e3ff61b26c"><span data-offset-key="72fc266117cd40f7a90f20e3ff61b26c:0"> method that implements </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-sequence" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f4786eb43a5d4c169412633744fac66b"><span data-offset-key="f4786eb43a5d4c169412633744fac66b:0">Sequence</span></span></a><span data-key="fadae7e145434e6c9fb8fa6e2b842752"><span data-offset-key="fadae7e145434e6c9fb8fa6e2b842752:0"> semantics.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5e8bdc21747a4895a234fd8dd69626b8"><span data-offset-key="5e8bdc21747a4895a234fd8dd69626b8:0">Iterables can be used in a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#for" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8ad4fa9fb1dc44d38a95b813310a2cb9"><span data-offset-key="8ad4fa9fb1dc44d38a95b813310a2cb9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">for</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5c83751a7c4b46339faf7757e46a38dd"><span data-offset-key="5c83751a7c4b46339faf7757e46a38dd:0"> loop and in many other places where a sequence is needed (</span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#zip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dfd1a06808fd413fae379e1a9e021e38"><span data-offset-key="dfd1a06808fd413fae379e1a9e021e38:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">zip()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b2516f588045454688561ac1d2187450"><span data-offset-key="b2516f588045454688561ac1d2187450:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#map" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c280eacb54a247898f03d50a75028cd1"><span data-offset-key="c280eacb54a247898f03d50a75028cd1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">map()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7f517822ccd644bdac7602da4c8af840"><span data-offset-key="7f517822ccd644bdac7602da4c8af840:0">, …). When an iterable object is passed as an argument to the built-in function </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#iter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f19d14deaa364af49a71215a63e57b94"><span data-offset-key="f19d14deaa364af49a71215a63e57b94:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">iter()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="43c6542ebf784240bf1da5ade1f022a0"><span data-offset-key="43c6542ebf784240bf1da5ade1f022a0:0">, it returns an iterator for the object. This iterator is good for one pass over the set of values. When using iterables, it is usually not necessary to call </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#iter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="69b87371fd0848609ddec780b319b354"><span data-offset-key="69b87371fd0848609ddec780b319b354:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">iter()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4f762ae232ed47ea956a0382c4bd0b17"><span data-offset-key="4f762ae232ed47ea956a0382c4bd0b17:0"> or deal with iterator objects yourself. The </span><span data-offset-key="4f762ae232ed47ea956a0382c4bd0b17:1">`for`</span><span data-offset-key="4f762ae232ed47ea956a0382c4bd0b17:2"> statement does that automatically for you, creating a temporary unnamed variable to hold the iterator for the duration of the loop. See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f9abc3efe1094ad99c2b74a092cc34ca"><span data-offset-key="f9abc3efe1094ad99c2b74a092cc34ca:0">iterator</span></span></a><span data-key="5c35f09217254a3391b450b63e8ca1a4"><span data-offset-key="5c35f09217254a3391b450b63e8ca1a4:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-sequence" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3355bd3656f040b78400b9df9e2e7286"><span data-offset-key="3355bd3656f040b78400b9df9e2e7286:0">sequence</span></span></a><span data-key="416fe08fd58349d2aafa41368a2d784b"><span data-offset-key="416fe08fd58349d2aafa41368a2d784b:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-generator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3759e374c965421a87d4223e4a4b52a4"><span data-offset-key="3759e374c965421a87d4223e4a4b52a4:0">generator</span></span></a><span data-key="c25712a4945d450fb8305023bc599b5f"><span data-offset-key="c25712a4945d450fb8305023bc599b5f:0">.iterator</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="89b4b24efa814de08ff27ea2763176ae"><span data-offset-key="89b4b24efa814de08ff27ea2763176ae:0">An object representing a stream of data. Repeated calls to the iterator’s </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#iterator.__next__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1b8423f1811d442bac6d3326654ed345"><span data-offset-key="1b8423f1811d442bac6d3326654ed345:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__next__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c61ad81a3f3742f0a3994d168a891234"><span data-offset-key="c61ad81a3f3742f0a3994d168a891234:0"> method (or passing it to the built-in function </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#next" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bfc80c1ebec54e4e87ea908b5962e5d6"><span data-offset-key="bfc80c1ebec54e4e87ea908b5962e5d6:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">next()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="fc2d5a116c6547e7baa16f3213a5da27"><span data-offset-key="fc2d5a116c6547e7baa16f3213a5da27:0">) return successive items in the stream. When no more data are available a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#StopIteration" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="11f28e3c5f754b24bf5e2464c87d166c"><span data-offset-key="11f28e3c5f754b24bf5e2464c87d166c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">StopIteration</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a46ddcd21b2a4ef4a4bc4d3abf3debbf"><span data-offset-key="a46ddcd21b2a4ef4a4bc4d3abf3debbf:0"> exception is raised instead. At this point, the iterator object is exhausted and any further calls to its </span><span data-offset-key="a46ddcd21b2a4ef4a4bc4d3abf3debbf:1">`__next__()`</span><span data-offset-key="a46ddcd21b2a4ef4a4bc4d3abf3debbf:2"> method just raise </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#StopIteration" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="beb9328dade04345ae63eaaad8162a29"><span data-offset-key="beb9328dade04345ae63eaaad8162a29:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">StopIteration</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eeacbde4a5eb48a79e50862f01ecc223"><span data-offset-key="eeacbde4a5eb48a79e50862f01ecc223:0"> again. Iterators are required to have an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__iter__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="41dd393677a64dd4b8288b0954a767db"><span data-offset-key="41dd393677a64dd4b8288b0954a767db:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__iter__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="89856631d33543858e88342921e333c7"><span data-offset-key="89856631d33543858e88342921e333c7:0"> method that returns the iterator object itself so every iterator is also iterable and may be used in most places where other iterables are accepted. One notable exception is code which attempts multiple iteration passes. A container object (such as a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a1773892dc134f21bc0fdc635b35c143"><span data-offset-key="a1773892dc134f21bc0fdc635b35c143:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="eb183104902640549c96cda0c3f3041d"><span data-offset-key="eb183104902640549c96cda0c3f3041d:0">) produces a fresh new iterator each time you pass it to the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#iter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="29d92864517745d683fba3c1221b5cec"><span data-offset-key="29d92864517745d683fba3c1221b5cec:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">iter()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9f21a287fa3a414bab6228da056c573c"><span data-offset-key="9f21a287fa3a414bab6228da056c573c:0"> function or use it in a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#for" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ded2258dbf314fa3a377daee1fa9a75e"><span data-offset-key="ded2258dbf314fa3a377daee1fa9a75e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">for</code></span></span></a><span data-key="25ddc68470cf40b6b70cd7ec145f470f"><span data-offset-key="25ddc68470cf40b6b70cd7ec145f470f:0"> loop. Attempting this with an iterator will just return the same exhausted iterator object used in the previous iteration pass, making it appear like an empty container.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fbf016c611ec49e2a274749aeef144e9"><span data-offset-key="fbf016c611ec49e2a274749aeef144e9:0">More information can be found in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typeiter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="87f688564d3f45fe9593ecacaa363829"><span data-offset-key="87f688564d3f45fe9593ecacaa363829:0">Iterator Types</span></span></a><span data-key="fe203600e39a4312b529428beea9b662"><span data-offset-key="fe203600e39a4312b529428beea9b662:0">.key function</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b64685e050d64b56873ee707a694cb5c"><span data-offset-key="b64685e050d64b56873ee707a694cb5c:0">A key function or collation function is a callable that returns a value used for sorting or ordering. For example, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/locale.html#locale.strxfrm" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dc171e391a9f4606b32067390353fcb9"><span data-offset-key="dc171e391a9f4606b32067390353fcb9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">locale.strxfrm()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="859776230138466da8a4bc86cd98cf9c"><span data-offset-key="859776230138466da8a4bc86cd98cf9c:0"> is used to produce a sort key that is aware of locale specific sort conventions.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e0f7719656b8406a97751f96fa75798d"><span data-offset-key="e0f7719656b8406a97751f96fa75798d:0">A number of tools in Python accept key functions to control how elements are ordered or grouped. They include </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#min" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="50f6da2245f94e4092c34a2fab46b0a4"><span data-offset-key="50f6da2245f94e4092c34a2fab46b0a4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">min()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="09922a863ca744f4981e3b4fe311ff4a"><span data-offset-key="09922a863ca744f4981e3b4fe311ff4a:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#max" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a430241dae2043b785d5af820d9d8f58"><span data-offset-key="a430241dae2043b785d5af820d9d8f58:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">max()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c4624abe87aa443da859d7a85a2055c3"><span data-offset-key="c4624abe87aa443da859d7a85a2055c3:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#sorted" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8fa2fc04ca514f1f9ed7386ed3f7aebe"><span data-offset-key="8fa2fc04ca514f1f9ed7386ed3f7aebe:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sorted()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0bcc27969077492392ef0e391264d467"><span data-offset-key="0bcc27969077492392ef0e391264d467:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list.sort" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cc2b9358bc854e7c856da4b38368be7b"><span data-offset-key="cc2b9358bc854e7c856da4b38368be7b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list.sort()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e12ce086fb75403bbe0c6e7defeccb85"><span data-offset-key="e12ce086fb75403bbe0c6e7defeccb85:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/heapq.html#heapq.merge" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c297363d25e0448a8ee48acbb2c2b479"><span data-offset-key="c297363d25e0448a8ee48acbb2c2b479:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">heapq.merge()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="cd99f170fb4a43f09d19985d8ce71881"><span data-offset-key="cd99f170fb4a43f09d19985d8ce71881:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/heapq.html#heapq.nsmallest" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="69dc5af81b9c4732a02d584764756ba5"><span data-offset-key="69dc5af81b9c4732a02d584764756ba5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">heapq.nsmallest()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="94d340d434014ee0ae9eff12533b9b16"><span data-offset-key="94d340d434014ee0ae9eff12533b9b16:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/heapq.html#heapq.nlargest" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="016fac9872064c45bec8a68942ee4be1"><span data-offset-key="016fac9872064c45bec8a68942ee4be1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">heapq.nlargest()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6e3839ed7c5545b5b6e04a9aa5a3fc8b"><span data-offset-key="6e3839ed7c5545b5b6e04a9aa5a3fc8b:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.groupby" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0b69a2f245ac444eb29b21900a63c65a"><span data-offset-key="0b69a2f245ac444eb29b21900a63c65a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itertools.groupby()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8c8d40d850d34c2eb7ee819a340c60ba"><span data-offset-key="8c8d40d850d34c2eb7ee819a340c60ba:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fb40c9257add40e2b6354d7880216a4c"><span data-offset-key="fb40c9257add40e2b6354d7880216a4c:0">There are several ways to create a key function. For example. the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str.lower" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="410bc679a4be4244bc39378bfcd09899"><span data-offset-key="410bc679a4be4244bc39378bfcd09899:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str.lower()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="84cc0bd0400d4450a993fcfbbaac176a"><span data-offset-key="84cc0bd0400d4450a993fcfbbaac176a:0"> method can serve as a key function for case insensitive sorts. Alternatively, a key function can be built from a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#lambda" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="107d0c6ef2814df5be29505aa8b911d8"><span data-offset-key="107d0c6ef2814df5be29505aa8b911d8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">lambda</code></span></span></a><span data-key="31eba94acb864d90a2476da14103192d"><span data-offset-key="31eba94acb864d90a2476da14103192d:0"> expression such as </span><span data-offset-key="31eba94acb864d90a2476da14103192d:1">`lambda r: (r[0], r[2])`</span><span data-offset-key="31eba94acb864d90a2476da14103192d:2">. Also, the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/operator.html#module-operator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cd722e09ec254fb29df1bb48ae87adff"><span data-offset-key="cd722e09ec254fb29df1bb48ae87adff:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">operator</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5a1c58a862354176b022f16b8c3f190e"><span data-offset-key="5a1c58a862354176b022f16b8c3f190e:0"> module provides three key function constructors: </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/operator.html#operator.attrgetter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="92f92fd81c5b45bdbb658e9ba7c3df6a"><span data-offset-key="92f92fd81c5b45bdbb658e9ba7c3df6a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">attrgetter()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e12ca9ad3e0f499c84828b6578126590"><span data-offset-key="e12ca9ad3e0f499c84828b6578126590:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/operator.html#operator.itemgetter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cb9bbf7dfa564286a2540e03b399f691"><span data-offset-key="cb9bbf7dfa564286a2540e03b399f691:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itemgetter()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="71f094797b3a47e6a4adbda8cf300baf"><span data-offset-key="71f094797b3a47e6a4adbda8cf300baf:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/operator.html#operator.methodcaller" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="61871f6a10dd4fb1a2d13c50470236d7"><span data-offset-key="61871f6a10dd4fb1a2d13c50470236d7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">methodcaller()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ce3cb2c444714cc2bb1ebb4699a00631"><span data-offset-key="ce3cb2c444714cc2bb1ebb4699a00631:0">. See the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/howto/sorting.html#sortinghowto" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ae7ce8f7af00414a98860723400b60e7"><span data-offset-key="ae7ce8f7af00414a98860723400b60e7:0">Sorting HOW TO</span></span></a><span data-key="cd90bc64ebbf439fa30ea89519dcd5cc"><span data-offset-key="cd90bc64ebbf439fa30ea89519dcd5cc:0"> for examples of how to create and use key functions.keyword argument</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4b5cc1b44d454cd3acba3d9a694e73f8"><span data-offset-key="4b5cc1b44d454cd3acba3d9a694e73f8:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-argument" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d22e2c6f939d499c8e217dfa688e9772"><span data-offset-key="d22e2c6f939d499c8e217dfa688e9772:0">argument</span></span></a><span data-key="a8807314f2d3429fb862fc4cbb1327b4"><span data-offset-key="a8807314f2d3429fb862fc4cbb1327b4:0">.lambda</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ada165ddd9c24fa59cac73e3be497721"><span data-offset-key="ada165ddd9c24fa59cac73e3be497721:0">An anonymous inline function consisting of a single </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-expression" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4c2707a9bed04b58970c5661d8249a66"><span data-offset-key="4c2707a9bed04b58970c5661d8249a66:0">expression</span></span></a><span data-key="d02e0778feb342bc91123edf208293e0"><span data-offset-key="d02e0778feb342bc91123edf208293e0:0"> which is evaluated when the function is called. The syntax to create a lambda function is </span><span data-offset-key="d02e0778feb342bc91123edf208293e0:1">`lambda [parameters]: expression`</span><span data-offset-key="d02e0778feb342bc91123edf208293e0:2">LBYL</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0b3d12b2c2f645c2a6669aefd1d8b02c"><span data-offset-key="0b3d12b2c2f645c2a6669aefd1d8b02c:0">Look before you leap. This coding style explicitly tests for pre-conditions before making calls or lookups. This style contrasts with the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-eafp" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1856f4fd5611469a931b97f62b9044b5"><span data-offset-key="1856f4fd5611469a931b97f62b9044b5:0">EAFP</span></span></a><span data-key="19763872ffb4477ab168dc257bf49bfa"><span data-offset-key="19763872ffb4477ab168dc257bf49bfa:0"> approach and is characterized by the presence of many </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#if" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4066c3613da24050942fe43bd01d6624"><span data-offset-key="4066c3613da24050942fe43bd01d6624:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">if</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ad2ab702473d4a62bcc5598f52673a6b"><span data-offset-key="ad2ab702473d4a62bcc5598f52673a6b:0"> statements.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a96b24b7146541f6b719a6e8f81dc8f1"><span data-offset-key="a96b24b7146541f6b719a6e8f81dc8f1:0">In a multi-threaded environment, the LBYL approach can risk introducing a race condition between “the looking” and “the leaping”. For example, the code, </span><span data-offset-key="a96b24b7146541f6b719a6e8f81dc8f1:1">`if key in mapping: return                                       mapping[key]`</span><span data-offset-key="a96b24b7146541f6b719a6e8f81dc8f1:2"> can fail if another thread removes </span><span data-offset-key="a96b24b7146541f6b719a6e8f81dc8f1:3">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="a96b24b7146541f6b719a6e8f81dc8f1:4"> from </span><span data-offset-key="a96b24b7146541f6b719a6e8f81dc8f1:5">*mapping*</span><span data-offset-key="a96b24b7146541f6b719a6e8f81dc8f1:6"> after the test, but before the lookup. This issue can be solved with locks or by using the EAFP approach.list</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1ba64a9075824a9394e15bacbf49bd20"><span data-offset-key="1ba64a9075824a9394e15bacbf49bd20:0">A built-in Python </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-sequence" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0599eed204dd4ba0ad0c29ce3b55d861"><span data-offset-key="0599eed204dd4ba0ad0c29ce3b55d861:0">sequence</span></span></a><span data-key="638dad83a2e24260a79179f82327754a"><span data-offset-key="638dad83a2e24260a79179f82327754a:0">. Despite its name it is more akin to an array in other languages than to a linked list since access to elements is O(1).list comprehension</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3c1eeb59fdf54c6a88599a2ad995d29a"><span data-offset-key="3c1eeb59fdf54c6a88599a2ad995d29a:0">A compact way to process all or part of the elements in a sequence and return a list with the results. </span><span data-offset-key="3c1eeb59fdf54c6a88599a2ad995d29a:1">`result = ['{:#04x}'.format(x)                                       for x in range(256) if x % 2 == 0]`</span><span data-offset-key="3c1eeb59fdf54c6a88599a2ad995d29a:2"> generates a list of strings containing even hex numbers (0x..) in the range from 0 to 255.
