The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#if" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6c97f493b93b488fa49320943e6ea15a"><span data-offset-key="6c97f493b93b488fa49320943e6ea15a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">if</code></span></span></a><span data-key="df2ac2072aab4a36befecfe4b824946c"><span data-offset-key="df2ac2072aab4a36befecfe4b824946c:0"> clause is optional. If omitted, all elements in </span><span data-offset-key="df2ac2072aab4a36befecfe4b824946c:1">`range(256)`</span><span data-offset-key="df2ac2072aab4a36befecfe4b824946c:2"> are processed.loader</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b5e96eed8004225bae7a132156bbab9"><span data-offset-key="9b5e96eed8004225bae7a132156bbab9:0">An object that loads a module. It must define a method named </span><span data-offset-key="9b5e96eed8004225bae7a132156bbab9:1">`load_module()`</span><span data-offset-key="9b5e96eed8004225bae7a132156bbab9:2">. A loader is typically returned by a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="16e056a0fb5e4dfda3917f97a31e382d"><span data-offset-key="16e056a0fb5e4dfda3917f97a31e382d:0">finder</span></span></a><span data-key="3acdaf58199e4d6c90d727acb3546b51"><span data-offset-key="3acdaf58199e4d6c90d727acb3546b51:0">. See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0302" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="81343234ee0940bbab1373d05c5f0225"><span data-offset-key="81343234ee0940bbab1373d05c5f0225:0"><strong>PEP 302</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="af15b1b3019d4eb4b02fb6b2ee12679d"><span data-offset-key="af15b1b3019d4eb4b02fb6b2ee12679d:0"> for details and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.Loader" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a5f80dd9eaa84510a68ec16599060d9c"><span data-offset-key="a5f80dd9eaa84510a68ec16599060d9c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.abc.Loader</code></span></span></a><span data-key="37f53b525e1146f986921e06e3663993"><span data-offset-key="37f53b525e1146f986921e06e3663993:0"> for an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-abstract-base-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="45ab5bf37fdf4779bab40f89491b257f"><span data-offset-key="45ab5bf37fdf4779bab40f89491b257f:0">abstract base class</span></span></a><span data-key="95c7b5b547e440418fd07ed9b3db0a80"><span data-offset-key="95c7b5b547e440418fd07ed9b3db0a80:0">.magic method</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eec41d1352b94de0b69ff705e9d7fd42"><span data-offset-key="eec41d1352b94de0b69ff705e9d7fd42:0">An informal synonym for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-special-method" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f42651ae89844d289963aa13d14de878"><span data-offset-key="f42651ae89844d289963aa13d14de878:0">special method</span></span></a><span data-key="13d28edb587945cfa88ee51a9157017f"><span data-offset-key="13d28edb587945cfa88ee51a9157017f:0">.mapping</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="759e4c6aca654de5a5b408291842453c"><span data-offset-key="759e4c6aca654de5a5b408291842453c:0">A container object that supports arbitrary key lookups and implements the methods specified in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.abc.html#collections.abc.Mapping" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cf49b0f17885451a8a9cede3218dcb27"><span data-offset-key="cf49b0f17885451a8a9cede3218dcb27:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">Mapping</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9fbe553bdc1a4b7cb8e24d15c2835ca5"><span data-offset-key="9fbe553bdc1a4b7cb8e24d15c2835ca5:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.abc.html#collections.abc.MutableMapping" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="80a4c389f6064a26ba53545182552f62"><span data-offset-key="80a4c389f6064a26ba53545182552f62:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">MutableMapping</code></span></span></a><span data-key="dc7f78681e4c4d16b35832948eaadf0b"><span data-offset-key="dc7f78681e4c4d16b35832948eaadf0b:0"> </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.abc.html#collections-abstract-base-classes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="71105d95f0a84e1784c326c26f80ede0"><span data-offset-key="71105d95f0a84e1784c326c26f80ede0:0">abstract base classes</span></span></a><span data-key="d7c0170e002c4bbb8de87440643aef71"><span data-offset-key="d7c0170e002c4bbb8de87440643aef71:0">. Examples include </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="28f9370067d946a7bc3a93f2f2ce4abd"><span data-offset-key="28f9370067d946a7bc3a93f2f2ce4abd:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="90dc9b8263e4497ca5107af1f013782a"><span data-offset-key="90dc9b8263e4497ca5107af1f013782a:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#collections.defaultdict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9e7d4ef72aa54a6287253f47dcdec0db"><span data-offset-key="9e7d4ef72aa54a6287253f47dcdec0db:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.defaultdict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="57dc176f86d04cc3826cedd0bf1c1d31"><span data-offset-key="57dc176f86d04cc3826cedd0bf1c1d31:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#collections.OrderedDict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="01be09b47a7045738ff9d4b218b08153"><span data-offset-key="01be09b47a7045738ff9d4b218b08153:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.OrderedDict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4c1decafdaa345dd87155aa97961361e"><span data-offset-key="4c1decafdaa345dd87155aa97961361e:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#collections.Counter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5024d79fecaf4c9c97ecadb1bc69644a"><span data-offset-key="5024d79fecaf4c9c97ecadb1bc69644a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.Counter</code></span></span></a><span data-key="054a6c17c7db45fb9cd78d1811a0f1bb"><span data-offset-key="054a6c17c7db45fb9cd78d1811a0f1bb:0">.meta path finder</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="927fa32c93464156beb22c82e739923c"><span data-offset-key="927fa32c93464156beb22c82e739923c:0">A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fbec37e0660d44f591731f2210d6c94c"><span data-offset-key="fbec37e0660d44f591731f2210d6c94c:0">finder</span></span></a><span data-key="45d095eee89349f2a6b05e5cffd9094f"><span data-offset-key="45d095eee89349f2a6b05e5cffd9094f:0"> returned by a search of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.meta_path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6840b45605d34716b2b18d1a4fd38e5d"><span data-offset-key="6840b45605d34716b2b18d1a4fd38e5d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.meta_path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e43241d080ac49cdabe79ca27685511e"><span data-offset-key="e43241d080ac49cdabe79ca27685511e:0">. Meta path finders are related to, but different from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cbaad2e9e73e4e05a75240a5754a0b32"><span data-offset-key="cbaad2e9e73e4e05a75240a5754a0b32:0">path entry finders</span></span></a><span data-key="131b136d76544b5583b25b92f8c68139"><span data-offset-key="131b136d76544b5583b25b92f8c68139:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b65d7d673b654e6fb06c5a468bd923f8"><span data-offset-key="b65d7d673b654e6fb06c5a468bd923f8:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a947af0389934bf6b27190d400f4d3ea"><span data-offset-key="a947af0389934bf6b27190d400f4d3ea:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.abc.MetaPathFinder</code></span></span></a><span data-key="2321e6e982db43b5a17f2b4f0940f8ff"><span data-offset-key="2321e6e982db43b5a17f2b4f0940f8ff:0"> for the methods that meta path finders implement.metaclass</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8d30cf0b423942e08b193c7950f8d3dc"><span data-offset-key="8d30cf0b423942e08b193c7950f8d3dc:0">The class of a class. Class definitions create a class name, a class dictionary, and a list of base classes. The metaclass is responsible for taking those three arguments and creating the class. Most object oriented programming languages provide a default implementation. What makes Python special is that it is possible to create custom metaclasses. Most users never need this tool, but when the need arises, metaclasses can provide powerful, elegant solutions. They have been used for logging attribute access, adding thread-safety, tracking object creation, implementing singletons, and many other tasks.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c5937558457e400f83c5b201530adda0"><span data-offset-key="c5937558457e400f83c5b201530adda0:0">More information can be found in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#metaclasses" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c4b605f9d04e4310b592fe7e9de4f83a"><span data-offset-key="c4b605f9d04e4310b592fe7e9de4f83a:0">Metaclasses</span></span></a><span data-key="8c72a2fb008840d498e9a3a7026c2f92"><span data-offset-key="8c72a2fb008840d498e9a3a7026c2f92:0">.method</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ff8aec8d15eb416e8fa0b7835b4484aa"><span data-offset-key="ff8aec8d15eb416e8fa0b7835b4484aa:0">A function which is defined inside a class body. If called as an attribute of an instance of that class, the method will get the instance object as its first </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-argument" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="956139eeb6f04b26861ecd6db8ddf17f"><span data-offset-key="956139eeb6f04b26861ecd6db8ddf17f:0">argument</span></span></a><span data-key="af02091f699b435c93f6990e4925c0a3"><span data-offset-key="af02091f699b435c93f6990e4925c0a3:0"> (which is usually called </span><span data-offset-key="af02091f699b435c93f6990e4925c0a3:1">`self`</span><span data-offset-key="af02091f699b435c93f6990e4925c0a3:2">). See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-function" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1c78379d38cb4b1292826a96a65e5844"><span data-offset-key="1c78379d38cb4b1292826a96a65e5844:0">function</span></span></a><span data-key="cbd92d34c3b640f28c393ff2330a579d"><span data-offset-key="cbd92d34c3b640f28c393ff2330a579d:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-nested-scope" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="09798af8edb14709b2a6f647d8ffb0cb"><span data-offset-key="09798af8edb14709b2a6f647d8ffb0cb:0">nested scope</span></span></a><span data-key="53c2c79a3543411197bce7b962e46fd7"><span data-offset-key="53c2c79a3543411197bce7b962e46fd7:0">.method resolution order</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ee5d90996b1d4fbdad42e424860c1db6"><span data-offset-key="ee5d90996b1d4fbdad42e424860c1db6:0">Method Resolution Order is the order in which base classes are searched for a member during lookup. See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/download/releases/2.3/mro/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e942c20e63a842b2828fa7dc410ee06e"><span data-offset-key="e942c20e63a842b2828fa7dc410ee06e:0">The Python 2.3 Method Resolution Order</span></span></a><span data-key="c61ed1b24731463f814548395923c199"><span data-offset-key="c61ed1b24731463f814548395923c199:0"> for details of the algorithm used by the Python interpreter since the 2.3 release.module</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9c5048366baa4dc7bb369b1ea647dbe8"><span data-offset-key="9c5048366baa4dc7bb369b1ea647dbe8:0">An object that serves as an organizational unit of Python code. Modules have a namespace containing arbitrary Python objects. Modules are loaded into Python by the process of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-importing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="47bc56fded864db3b8b573e4ab436100"><span data-offset-key="47bc56fded864db3b8b573e4ab436100:0">importing</span></span></a><span data-key="96dc4eee89c8482ab49e4b38537a6224"><span data-offset-key="96dc4eee89c8482ab49e4b38537a6224:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1ac652e4f62e47ccbae8b1f5f920dca5"><span data-offset-key="1ac652e4f62e47ccbae8b1f5f920dca5:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="261f7a8c3fe7442ba2d2e621a6a40105"><span data-offset-key="261f7a8c3fe7442ba2d2e621a6a40105:0">package</span></span></a><span data-key="7263032b8c8f43e59fb26ef8809f2fd4"><span data-offset-key="7263032b8c8f43e59fb26ef8809f2fd4:0">.module spec</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1c6aecc149a840918459c2a72675f77f"><span data-offset-key="1c6aecc149a840918459c2a72675f77f:0">A namespace containing the import-related information used to load a module. An instance of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.machinery.ModuleSpec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9e427e2fdcc04529957b6c90f520b7b4"><span data-offset-key="9e427e2fdcc04529957b6c90f520b7b4:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.machinery.ModuleSpec</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e67633b5d9884874affa1af61b6c227f"><span data-offset-key="e67633b5d9884874affa1af61b6c227f:0">.MRO</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="459486baba82494f9b948a6f3c03d6d9"><span data-offset-key="459486baba82494f9b948a6f3c03d6d9:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-method-resolution-order" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ac4d3bd7fa6e4fd29dee39969d912dd2"><span data-offset-key="ac4d3bd7fa6e4fd29dee39969d912dd2:0">method resolution order</span></span></a><span data-key="1a028aae14b846f7b2375e180fc1d969"><span data-offset-key="1a028aae14b846f7b2375e180fc1d969:0">.mutable</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ae79b1f3362b452fb037fb0bfe8e9a21"><span data-offset-key="ae79b1f3362b452fb037fb0bfe8e9a21:0">Mutable objects can change their value but keep their </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#id" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6362536deeab4f41bb9ed633ace32afb"><span data-offset-key="6362536deeab4f41bb9ed633ace32afb:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">id()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="833d60fc7714411cbf29cbce5ace24c3"><span data-offset-key="833d60fc7714411cbf29cbce5ace24c3:0">. See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-immutable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c6cfdf589ec544a0b5ef31eb2426090e"><span data-offset-key="c6cfdf589ec544a0b5ef31eb2426090e:0">immutable</span></span></a><span data-key="5affe179fac64bb0acf9641ee3849186"><span data-offset-key="5affe179fac64bb0acf9641ee3849186:0">.named tuple</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="13371f0158e2400a91134bf89fffab8b"><span data-offset-key="13371f0158e2400a91134bf89fffab8b:0">The term “named tuple” applies to any type or class that inherits from tuple and whose indexable elements are also accessible using named attributes. The type or class may have other features as well.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="83d671293f14464dbf4d465db2979ab9"><span data-offset-key="83d671293f14464dbf4d465db2979ab9:0">Several built-in types are named tuples, including the values returned by </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/time.html#time.localtime" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e5f87294c9a440e8936320bb6ba85244"><span data-offset-key="e5f87294c9a440e8936320bb6ba85244:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">time.localtime()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d623d22a9be146cc864a16c31e3dfd0d"><span data-offset-key="d623d22a9be146cc864a16c31e3dfd0d:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.stat" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="51b3b227cf7e4979ac6ca0b01ec68942"><span data-offset-key="51b3b227cf7e4979ac6ca0b01ec68942:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.stat()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="971b286804dd461c86a4fa45d43056a1"><span data-offset-key="971b286804dd461c86a4fa45d43056a1:0">. Another example is </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.float_info" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="91c9f2ef7d3944099b9528ad8de7bae9"><span data-offset-key="91c9f2ef7d3944099b9528ad8de7bae9:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.float_info</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4be547e20efb483782b1085efa6945df"><span data-offset-key="4be547e20efb483782b1085efa6945df:0">:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> sys.float_info[1]                   # indexed access1024>>> sys.float_info.max_exp              # named field access1024>>> isinstance(sys.float_info, tuple)   # kind of tupleTrue

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7a25287e21ba497ba6fb3b824927ce45"><span data-offset-key="7a25287e21ba497ba6fb3b824927ce45:0">Some named tuples are built-in types (such as the above examples). Alternatively, a named tuple can be created from a regular class definition that inherits from </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0ad583d88df14e61992981f93455ea0d"><span data-offset-key="0ad583d88df14e61992981f93455ea0d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tuple</code></span></span></a><span data-key="82ed0df5d66846e48caece8fa8ec37ba"><span data-offset-key="82ed0df5d66846e48caece8fa8ec37ba:0"> and that defines named fields. Such a class can be written by hand or it can be created with the factory function </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#collections.namedtuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2779cee7f90f481cbda1bd3d3e394220"><span data-offset-key="2779cee7f90f481cbda1bd3d3e394220:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.namedtuple()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ea01d0d3f0024ea6a600e98a60b8fedd"><span data-offset-key="ea01d0d3f0024ea6a600e98a60b8fedd:0">. The latter technique also adds some extra methods that may not be found in hand-written or built-in named tuples.namespace</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bb5c6593f83c45738b159dc6f357d675"><span data-offset-key="bb5c6593f83c45738b159dc6f357d675:0">The place where a variable is stored. Namespaces are implemented as dictionaries. There are the local, global and built-in namespaces as well as nested namespaces in objects (in methods). Namespaces support modularity by preventing naming conflicts. For instance, the functions </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4ec274f92620451c85f6a32eb957d10c"><span data-offset-key="4ec274f92620451c85f6a32eb957d10c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">builtins.open</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7e8529ae84e9431992ee85e9fe1acd93"><span data-offset-key="7e8529ae84e9431992ee85e9fe1acd93:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c4ec1cdd52004df6920c2a7bb35b1972"><span data-offset-key="c4ec1cdd52004df6920c2a7bb35b1972:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.open()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c469539bcb5e4bea81cb96e23ecc55ce"><span data-offset-key="c469539bcb5e4bea81cb96e23ecc55ce:0"> are distinguished by their namespaces. Namespaces also aid readability and maintainability by making it clear which module implements a function. For instance, writing </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/random.html#random.seed" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1e4dae5138514887803ad6f86f3ea89c"><span data-offset-key="1e4dae5138514887803ad6f86f3ea89c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">random.seed()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9b55b96e586349d09975a05eb5a405c8"><span data-offset-key="9b55b96e586349d09975a05eb5a405c8:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.islice" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="07057e3bc4f2419dbf374aa7f2e4f971"><span data-offset-key="07057e3bc4f2419dbf374aa7f2e4f971:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itertools.islice()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f3a863b37e094d0e8883ee77fd33a541"><span data-offset-key="f3a863b37e094d0e8883ee77fd33a541:0"> makes it clear that those functions are implemented by the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/random.html#module-random" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b4b3dc79a9aa41ec96f6f38204daa790"><span data-offset-key="b4b3dc79a9aa41ec96f6f38204daa790:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">random</code></span></span></a><span data-key="d0b02f9ef0bc4b0f9a970cebed284309"><span data-offset-key="d0b02f9ef0bc4b0f9a970cebed284309:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#module-itertools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d6126e98a781495caf70d15c1ed92524"><span data-offset-key="d6126e98a781495caf70d15c1ed92524:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">itertools</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b21d331add3e485ca010553d011c394f"><span data-offset-key="b21d331add3e485ca010553d011c394f:0"> modules, respectively.namespace package</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b5d94b10ea0f435489fd7dcf187d0bfc"><span data-offset-key="b5d94b10ea0f435489fd7dcf187d0bfc:0">A </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0420" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="48991b36cec5410bba764bec546476ce"><span data-offset-key="48991b36cec5410bba764bec546476ce:0"><strong>PEP 420</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="94c6c16af4624bfc9a0597b5caf90961"><span data-offset-key="94c6c16af4624bfc9a0597b5caf90961:0"> </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0cf873085a8145dcbf77190d7a361d5a"><span data-offset-key="0cf873085a8145dcbf77190d7a361d5a:0">package</span></span></a><span data-key="f63c8c888a514e1c87edeabfdff20f21"><span data-offset-key="f63c8c888a514e1c87edeabfdff20f21:0"> which serves only as a container for subpackages. Namespace packages may have no physical representation, and specifically are not like a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-regular-package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6966399b2b564f33a9d5cda20cc94a8c"><span data-offset-key="6966399b2b564f33a9d5cda20cc94a8c:0">regular package</span></span></a><span data-key="af9b16bdbf7c472cb8f273e7830a6bdc"><span data-offset-key="af9b16bdbf7c472cb8f273e7830a6bdc:0"> because they have no </span><span data-offset-key="af9b16bdbf7c472cb8f273e7830a6bdc:1">`__init__.py`</span><span data-offset-key="af9b16bdbf7c472cb8f273e7830a6bdc:2"> file.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cd453e79e6ff464f8fff96c094648816"><span data-offset-key="cd453e79e6ff464f8fff96c094648816:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="caec1bb955b34637984f3fb17cb8d122"><span data-offset-key="caec1bb955b34637984f3fb17cb8d122:0">module</span></span></a><span data-key="545d7387d97b443d878b07ecd0079036"><span data-offset-key="545d7387d97b443d878b07ecd0079036:0">.nested scope</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2fccf33f12f3470e9fa9fff08bbfb7e7"><span data-offset-key="2fccf33f12f3470e9fa9fff08bbfb7e7:0">The ability to refer to a variable in an enclosing definition. For instance, a function defined inside another function can refer to variables in the outer function. Note that nested scopes by default work only for reference and not for assignment. Local variables both read and write in the innermost scope. Likewise, global variables read and write to the global namespace. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#nonlocal" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7418d8d72b9a4f06a5729f13ca3ad375"><span data-offset-key="7418d8d72b9a4f06a5729f13ca3ad375:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">nonlocal</code></span></span></a><span data-key="dda7ebfcee2f4de4819ad716dd231c0d"><span data-offset-key="dda7ebfcee2f4de4819ad716dd231c0d:0"> allows writing to outer scopes.new-style class</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0ea66d21d32649bfbbb6ff78b568271b"><span data-offset-key="0ea66d21d32649bfbbb6ff78b568271b:0">Old name for the flavor of classes now used for all class objects. In earlier Python versions, only new-style classes could use Python’s newer, versatile features like </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__slots__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d42a1671b56144169409d17d91df6b56"><span data-offset-key="d42a1671b56144169409d17d91df6b56:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__slots__</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6dd2a46f837d4cccb1e71e43b6eea8c5"><span data-offset-key="6dd2a46f837d4cccb1e71e43b6eea8c5:0">, descriptors, properties, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getattribute__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="080dfd916ea8451a8669f3f684129a28"><span data-offset-key="080dfd916ea8451a8669f3f684129a28:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getattribute__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a15fa7699e114c848c934e4c5094b618"><span data-offset-key="a15fa7699e114c848c934e4c5094b618:0">, class methods, and static methods.object</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9007f142cdb94941bb548b484647b322"><span data-offset-key="9007f142cdb94941bb548b484647b322:0">Any data with state (attributes or value) and defined behavior (methods). Also the ultimate base class of any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-new-style-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1707963651414f88a86ccef8a7246d46"><span data-offset-key="1707963651414f88a86ccef8a7246d46:0">new-style class</span></span></a><span data-key="e22f16a362af4db2b2eaf02536a3d628"><span data-offset-key="e22f16a362af4db2b2eaf02536a3d628:0">.package</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c4c24b4b84fd4ba49b1c5e370aa04c47"><span data-offset-key="c4c24b4b84fd4ba49b1c5e370aa04c47:0">A Python </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e8e3731282dc4773b81e09b06820f58c"><span data-offset-key="e8e3731282dc4773b81e09b06820f58c:0">module</span></span></a><span data-key="acce5cdec2eb42afacf04eb2ff204b10"><span data-offset-key="acce5cdec2eb42afacf04eb2ff204b10:0"> which can contain submodules or recursively, subpackages. Technically, a package is a Python module with an </span><span data-offset-key="acce5cdec2eb42afacf04eb2ff204b10:1">`__path__`</span><span data-offset-key="acce5cdec2eb42afacf04eb2ff204b10:2"> attribute.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6c4b5cfec339404aa93830722980e469"><span data-offset-key="6c4b5cfec339404aa93830722980e469:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-regular-package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5e4cd6a3c58246c690e06f8736136c35"><span data-offset-key="5e4cd6a3c58246c690e06f8736136c35:0">regular package</span></span></a><span data-key="a691d2efac474e8b9ff25a55602664f0"><span data-offset-key="a691d2efac474e8b9ff25a55602664f0:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-namespace-package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="39aac7604ad540879dc3c774b71a260a"><span data-offset-key="39aac7604ad540879dc3c774b71a260a:0">namespace package</span></span></a><span data-key="6b1c6dcb1d24417cbded11f408ef9b32"><span data-offset-key="6b1c6dcb1d24417cbded11f408ef9b32:0">.parameter</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="237b5547061543c99fb3c8f9e5d5b60d"><span data-offset-key="237b5547061543c99fb3c8f9e5d5b60d:0">A named entity in a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-function" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6a2039356565430cb8afc4c2e947ba5f"><span data-offset-key="6a2039356565430cb8afc4c2e947ba5f:0">function</span></span></a><span data-key="3a946f7f9dca48a280203170a83a12e9"><span data-offset-key="3a946f7f9dca48a280203170a83a12e9:0"> (or method) definition that specifies an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-argument" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b3e876dce8594a28912a1fe662eccdd7"><span data-offset-key="b3e876dce8594a28912a1fe662eccdd7:0">argument</span></span></a><span data-key="b9e6835d889645e789a72ed322f1f3e0"><span data-offset-key="b9e6835d889645e789a72ed322f1f3e0:0"> (or in some cases, arguments) that the function can accept. There are five kinds of parameter:</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="66a1d0efa2b14154a62e4e349622326e"><span data-offset-key="66a1d0efa2b14154a62e4e349622326e:0">*positional-or-keyword*</span><span data-offset-key="66a1d0efa2b14154a62e4e349622326e:1">: specifies an argument that can be passed either </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-argument" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c1b2ea933b134188a0079f5f547f6f47"><span data-offset-key="c1b2ea933b134188a0079f5f547f6f47:0">positionally</span></span></a><span data-key="232e418adad54b73b79429cd00d1b1b9"><span data-offset-key="232e418adad54b73b79429cd00d1b1b9:0"> or as a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-argument" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="347c3bcbfaa24f698e7c9e379077726f"><span data-offset-key="347c3bcbfaa24f698e7c9e379077726f:0">keyword argument</span></span></a><span data-key="41d7c96c29084e69b0c79a9738f07c24"><span data-offset-key="41d7c96c29084e69b0c79a9738f07c24:0">. This is the default kind of parameter, for example </span><span data-offset-key="41d7c96c29084e69b0c79a9738f07c24:1">*foo*</span><span data-offset-key="41d7c96c29084e69b0c79a9738f07c24:2"> and </span><span data-offset-key="41d7c96c29084e69b0c79a9738f07c24:3">*bar*</span><span data-offset-key="41d7c96c29084e69b0c79a9738f07c24:4"> in the following:</span></span></span>

        def func(foo, bar=None): ...

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e"><span data-offset-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e:0">*positional-only*</span><span data-offset-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e:1">: specifies an argument that can be supplied only by position. Positional-only parameters can be defined by including a </span><span data-offset-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e:2">`/`</span><span data-offset-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e:3"> character in the parameter list of the function definition after them, for example </span><span data-offset-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e:4">*posonly1*</span><span data-offset-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e:5"> and </span><span data-offset-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e:6">*posonly2*</span><span data-offset-key="22f83e4f0d9745559ed8b3734b7b567e:7"> in the following:</span></span></span>

        def func(posonly1, posonly2, /, positional_or_keyword): ...

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154"><span data-offset-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154:0">*keyword-only*</span><span data-offset-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154:1">: specifies an argument that can be supplied only by keyword. Keyword-only parameters can be defined by including a single var-positional parameter or bare </span><span data-offset-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154:2">`*`</span><span data-offset-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154:3"> in the parameter list of the function definition before them, for example </span><span data-offset-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154:4">*kw\_only1*</span><span data-offset-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154:5"> and </span><span data-offset-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154:6">*kw\_only2*</span><span data-offset-key="96b013143d1b4c5b861a0d1d28be2154:7"> in the following:</span></span></span>

        def func(arg, *, kw_only1, kw_only2): ...

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f1a00fe1b31e4cce8b0397ca89d9ef84"><span data-offset-key="f1a00fe1b31e4cce8b0397ca89d9ef84:0">*var-positional*</span><span data-offset-key="f1a00fe1b31e4cce8b0397ca89d9ef84:1">: specifies that an arbitrary sequence of positional arguments can be provided (in addition to any positional arguments already accepted by other parameters). Such a parameter can be defined by prepending the parameter name with </span><span data-offset-key="f1a00fe1b31e4cce8b0397ca89d9ef84:2">`*`</span><span data-offset-key="f1a00fe1b31e4cce8b0397ca89d9ef84:3">, for example </span><span data-offset-key="f1a00fe1b31e4cce8b0397ca89d9ef84:4">*args*</span><span data-offset-key="f1a00fe1b31e4cce8b0397ca89d9ef84:5"> in the following:</span></span></span>

        def func(*args, **kwargs): ...

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="986400f7c96d4cacbddd06d07b5dbe22"><span data-offset-key="986400f7c96d4cacbddd06d07b5dbe22:0">*var-keyword*</span><span data-offset-key="986400f7c96d4cacbddd06d07b5dbe22:1">: specifies that arbitrarily many keyword arguments can be provided (in addition to any keyword arguments already accepted by other parameters). Such a parameter can be defined by prepending the parameter name with </span><span data-offset-key="986400f7c96d4cacbddd06d07b5dbe22:2">`**`</span><span data-offset-key="986400f7c96d4cacbddd06d07b5dbe22:3">, for example </span><span data-offset-key="986400f7c96d4cacbddd06d07b5dbe22:4">*kwargs*</span><span data-offset-key="986400f7c96d4cacbddd06d07b5dbe22:5"> in the example above.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a30300803b4840049b27f2b0e38f5048"><span data-offset-key="a30300803b4840049b27f2b0e38f5048:0">Parameters can specify both optional and required arguments, as well as default values for some optional arguments.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f1eb16a193f742e988c79e75b536fe6e"><span data-offset-key="f1eb16a193f742e988c79e75b536fe6e:0">See also the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-argument" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b007607d2f5e45d1bd2ffc8414470e62"><span data-offset-key="b007607d2f5e45d1bd2ffc8414470e62:0">argument</span></span></a><span data-key="7c67c256a6294f70bbb78d8e4d0b3bb5"><span data-offset-key="7c67c256a6294f70bbb78d8e4d0b3bb5:0"> glossary entry, the FAQ question on </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/faq/programming.html#faq-argument-vs-parameter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ebb0b088355641059875ddd74d2d7092"><span data-offset-key="ebb0b088355641059875ddd74d2d7092:0">the difference between arguments and parameters</span></span></a><span data-key="5e3c1056f9174968907c3fa651061cb4"><span data-offset-key="5e3c1056f9174968907c3fa651061cb4:0">, the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/inspect.html#inspect.Parameter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="968a603384174adb8e5ceb55e13ca966"><span data-offset-key="968a603384174adb8e5ceb55e13ca966:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">inspect.Parameter</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7327b012d3fd40488bf85524d702304c"><span data-offset-key="7327b012d3fd40488bf85524d702304c:0"> class, the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#function" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="13a5896ce0784d81ab06fdda9ced74bf"><span data-offset-key="13a5896ce0784d81ab06fdda9ced74bf:0">Function definitions</span></span></a><span data-key="74c55ac700cd42318940a312b0fb8687"><span data-offset-key="74c55ac700cd42318940a312b0fb8687:0"> section, and </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0362" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dd655e54995f44c2a1e7f2a11ebbbb01"><span data-offset-key="dd655e54995f44c2a1e7f2a11ebbbb01:0"><strong>PEP 362</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="40e893d205284deba368432a34f1251e"><span data-offset-key="40e893d205284deba368432a34f1251e:0">.path entry</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="25e44ce865294580934c059771f13804"><span data-offset-key="25e44ce865294580934c059771f13804:0">A single location on the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="efddae3e34c24ac298b28aae9d99f5ea"><span data-offset-key="efddae3e34c24ac298b28aae9d99f5ea:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="35a46eddbc994ecc956d91941a2271b0"><span data-offset-key="35a46eddbc994ecc956d91941a2271b0:0"> which the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-based-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3ad29a7d17e14e1294c15f2ab23ac431"><span data-offset-key="3ad29a7d17e14e1294c15f2ab23ac431:0">path based finder</span></span></a><span data-key="e2968a23ec254f32a425790efab0d5f1"><span data-offset-key="e2968a23ec254f32a425790efab0d5f1:0"> consults to find modules for importing.path entry finder</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="513b78ce918a47f1925578adbe49c85a"><span data-offset-key="513b78ce918a47f1925578adbe49c85a:0">A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4b5ed4158ac74ababff4bcf1beb3f268"><span data-offset-key="4b5ed4158ac74ababff4bcf1beb3f268:0">finder</span></span></a><span data-key="5a11e3ade4944b49b87c0cc04f65e329"><span data-offset-key="5a11e3ade4944b49b87c0cc04f65e329:0"> returned by a callable on </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.path_hooks" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4c8d80348bb947b699c1afcd01036cda"><span data-offset-key="4c8d80348bb947b699c1afcd01036cda:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path_hooks</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b2d3ce10bb6343ffbf17cb1587d49a06"><span data-offset-key="b2d3ce10bb6343ffbf17cb1587d49a06:0"> (i.e. a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-hook" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7b5a43fa162849c380e0c71de7dd759a"><span data-offset-key="7b5a43fa162849c380e0c71de7dd759a:0">path entry hook</span></span></a><span data-key="cda63e26002646309a7ad3ae74eef539"><span data-offset-key="cda63e26002646309a7ad3ae74eef539:0">) which knows how to locate modules given a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="605822cdb5894a5abdb79147890d895c"><span data-offset-key="605822cdb5894a5abdb79147890d895c:0">path entry</span></span></a><span data-key="c994e974eb524d8e8e8932a6962b00ee"><span data-offset-key="c994e974eb524d8e8e8932a6962b00ee:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4f21582110104bfe86645426a66f7fcb"><span data-offset-key="4f21582110104bfe86645426a66f7fcb:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/importlib.html#importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d61b21d98f4742fabad9bbda373dff9a"><span data-offset-key="d61b21d98f4742fabad9bbda373dff9a:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">importlib.abc.PathEntryFinder</code></span></span></a><span data-key="4878a3dc24284d31850efcde47e94389"><span data-offset-key="4878a3dc24284d31850efcde47e94389:0"> for the methods that path entry finders implement.path entry hook</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="35157564529447b8a349969eb9bc0e8d"><span data-offset-key="35157564529447b8a349969eb9bc0e8d:0">A callable on the </span><span data-offset-key="35157564529447b8a349969eb9bc0e8d:1">`sys.path_hook`</span><span data-offset-key="35157564529447b8a349969eb9bc0e8d:2"> list which returns a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fb9bbffeba884eb9b86a02cca970de6c"><span data-offset-key="fb9bbffeba884eb9b86a02cca970de6c:0">path entry finder</span></span></a><span data-key="fe7273dbf505472e991dac38e335dcc5"><span data-offset-key="fe7273dbf505472e991dac38e335dcc5:0"> if it knows how to find modules on a specific </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-entry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="040a8ca4b64a48ed92effa56238e71ae"><span data-offset-key="040a8ca4b64a48ed92effa56238e71ae:0">path entry</span></span></a><span data-key="9afd697be79c481a92782566517bfae1"><span data-offset-key="9afd697be79c481a92782566517bfae1:0">.path based finder</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="40f9c79a00f6493ba77530078dcb6249"><span data-offset-key="40f9c79a00f6493ba77530078dcb6249:0">One of the default </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-meta-path-finder" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8046af721006423e9fa65d0fa3e43a12"><span data-offset-key="8046af721006423e9fa65d0fa3e43a12:0">meta path finders</span></span></a><span data-key="8eb213e3194a42dfafedd8ab3b1a8d80"><span data-offset-key="8eb213e3194a42dfafedd8ab3b1a8d80:0"> which searches an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-import-path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="734a1c4e22264b80add9a23100a6b869"><span data-offset-key="734a1c4e22264b80add9a23100a6b869:0">import path</span></span></a><span data-key="fa1d1df88ee247e79cffded126e0fb89"><span data-offset-key="fa1d1df88ee247e79cffded126e0fb89:0"> for modules.path-like object</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="85bda8e3015c449d9e7394981fa40c44"><span data-offset-key="85bda8e3015c449d9e7394981fa40c44:0">An object representing a file system path. A path-like object is either a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e4c00954981a47d28267e48f3b8c88f1"><span data-offset-key="e4c00954981a47d28267e48f3b8c88f1:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="359c5c90b29c43ef8b4b4ef3a8f20c9e"><span data-offset-key="359c5c90b29c43ef8b4b4ef3a8f20c9e:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="518220e3c4874ceaaf8b98323bd793fc"><span data-offset-key="518220e3c4874ceaaf8b98323bd793fc:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a019beb5782343058bf4a743b41dccf1"><span data-offset-key="a019beb5782343058bf4a743b41dccf1:0"> object representing a path, or an object implementing the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.PathLike" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="33e505beefa0407b947d08dbead92141"><span data-offset-key="33e505beefa0407b947d08dbead92141:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.PathLike</code></span></span></a><span data-key="12f364c91fd14d2fbd697e3653186f94"><span data-offset-key="12f364c91fd14d2fbd697e3653186f94:0"> protocol. An object that supports the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.PathLike" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8e6177e8ae634e59b540a189d59c3bad"><span data-offset-key="8e6177e8ae634e59b540a189d59c3bad:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.PathLike</code></span></span></a><span data-key="478ec819d8334653bfb2fa18f38112b0"><span data-offset-key="478ec819d8334653bfb2fa18f38112b0:0"> protocol can be converted to a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7d389cb4d76c4969995df88e2a2df11c"><span data-offset-key="7d389cb4d76c4969995df88e2a2df11c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="da34775117e84d9ba37f38cc38abecf3"><span data-offset-key="da34775117e84d9ba37f38cc38abecf3:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="be54e964cf5e4f81b52e4a35b85ee096"><span data-offset-key="be54e964cf5e4f81b52e4a35b85ee096:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9387f668f60c468ca8b0509dd90e70e1"><span data-offset-key="9387f668f60c468ca8b0509dd90e70e1:0"> file system path by calling the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.fspath" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6dd73795991c45a8b4a8bcc790601c77"><span data-offset-key="6dd73795991c45a8b4a8bcc790601c77:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.fspath()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="46eecf9d96ae40519ac8256b4b56568a"><span data-offset-key="46eecf9d96ae40519ac8256b4b56568a:0"> function; </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.fsdecode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7010eb8caa7f4654b02f81c8417320ed"><span data-offset-key="7010eb8caa7f4654b02f81c8417320ed:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.fsdecode()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ec92c9e0e6524b36905d75f31f7575e6"><span data-offset-key="ec92c9e0e6524b36905d75f31f7575e6:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.fsencode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="08ff048cf8c54ff1b1f327ca4a9c856b"><span data-offset-key="08ff048cf8c54ff1b1f327ca4a9c856b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">os.fsencode()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="370bc97141cb43e7b58b3bb670faa15c"><span data-offset-key="370bc97141cb43e7b58b3bb670faa15c:0"> can be used to guarantee a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1660b83bf40143a8be9da3de2c4b8f0c"><span data-offset-key="1660b83bf40143a8be9da3de2c4b8f0c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="1d0275499fe349bab530df65587f71b4"><span data-offset-key="1d0275499fe349bab530df65587f71b4:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="96ab16232c64494e9640a6fe2640144b"><span data-offset-key="96ab16232c64494e9640a6fe2640144b:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f4cd8bd5411145fdba18160e096de300"><span data-offset-key="f4cd8bd5411145fdba18160e096de300:0"> result instead, respectively. Introduced by </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0519" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="efa0d711c36a44dcaa77519a0a9d4cd2"><span data-offset-key="efa0d711c36a44dcaa77519a0a9d4cd2:0"><strong>PEP 519</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="e5d6ef0590ff43e2bf8b1be1e2226ab8"><span data-offset-key="e5d6ef0590ff43e2bf8b1be1e2226ab8:0">.PEP</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7ee7f4f562fc48a5836cfc41558b401a"><span data-offset-key="7ee7f4f562fc48a5836cfc41558b401a:0">Python Enhancement Proposal. A PEP is a design document providing information to the Python community, or describing a new feature for Python or its processes or environment. PEPs should provide a concise technical specification and a rationale for proposed features.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1e8f1b74c11940298256d3fecdcf3429"><span data-offset-key="1e8f1b74c11940298256d3fecdcf3429:0">PEPs are intended to be the primary mechanisms for proposing major new features, for collecting community input on an issue, and for documenting the design decisions that have gone into Python. The PEP author is responsible for building consensus within the community and documenting dissenting opinions.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="25f94ce3026a4a2ea87b2a5ce4f990d0"><span data-offset-key="25f94ce3026a4a2ea87b2a5ce4f990d0:0">See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0001" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="153d15d71be24a668cf937c699e051d7"><span data-offset-key="153d15d71be24a668cf937c699e051d7:0"><strong>PEP 1</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="88c63c256b76471297cd8dc2ce570ebf"><span data-offset-key="88c63c256b76471297cd8dc2ce570ebf:0">.portion</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="05a1238212504932b744fca612ac5de2"><span data-offset-key="05a1238212504932b744fca612ac5de2:0">A set of files in a single directory (possibly stored in a zip file) that contribute to a namespace package, as defined in </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0420" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c1d55a727cdd41fd80611f9c7c37a06e"><span data-offset-key="c1d55a727cdd41fd80611f9c7c37a06e:0"><strong>PEP 420</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="12923b79fc5f44d0be05dbc85a7270c4"><span data-offset-key="12923b79fc5f44d0be05dbc85a7270c4:0">.positional argument</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="943f557874d34b4689926cc45dba1b22"><span data-offset-key="943f557874d34b4689926cc45dba1b22:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-argument" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b1d3fcd71c22465c935ce54c761873a9"><span data-offset-key="b1d3fcd71c22465c935ce54c761873a9:0">argument</span></span></a><span data-key="b507f8181ba54432a3e2dd6074d8d63e"><span data-offset-key="b507f8181ba54432a3e2dd6074d8d63e:0">.provisional API</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="80aa56ea95294425acc967eaa7458856"><span data-offset-key="80aa56ea95294425acc967eaa7458856:0">A provisional API is one which has been deliberately excluded from the standard library’s backwards compatibility guarantees. While major changes to such interfaces are not expected, as long as they are marked provisional, backwards incompatible changes (up to and including removal of the interface) may occur if deemed necessary by core developers. Such changes will not be made gratuitously – they will occur only if serious fundamental flaws are uncovered that were missed prior to the inclusion of the API.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fc5f8f9dd7a5474dbe19a4ba45d82faf"><span data-offset-key="fc5f8f9dd7a5474dbe19a4ba45d82faf:0">Even for provisional APIs, backwards incompatible changes are seen as a “solution of last resort” - every attempt will still be made to find a backwards compatible resolution to any identified problems.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="39af2fed4b7d4af0b0d2983f34da1569"><span data-offset-key="39af2fed4b7d4af0b0d2983f34da1569:0">This process allows the standard library to continue to evolve over time, without locking in problematic design errors for extended periods of time. See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0411" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9c201d7de617499e9f012e817e59ebe4"><span data-offset-key="9c201d7de617499e9f012e817e59ebe4:0"><strong>PEP 411</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="ce82ce15fa3146faac9063c94d4e2698"><span data-offset-key="ce82ce15fa3146faac9063c94d4e2698:0"> for more details.provisional package</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="948e52178dac4fa68f95249489fad7c8"><span data-offset-key="948e52178dac4fa68f95249489fad7c8:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-provisional-api" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9c4b755760844308b3424289b152b285"><span data-offset-key="9c4b755760844308b3424289b152b285:0">provisional API</span></span></a><span data-key="274412c041e64765995439fdc32b5fa9"><span data-offset-key="274412c041e64765995439fdc32b5fa9:0">.Python 3000</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="536a748f35704c0baa20a2015e6aa632"><span data-offset-key="536a748f35704c0baa20a2015e6aa632:0">Nickname for the Python 3.x release line (coined long ago when the release of version 3 was something in the distant future.) This is also abbreviated “Py3k”.Pythonic</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ceb8ad98593e42f09023e12909922711"><span data-offset-key="ceb8ad98593e42f09023e12909922711:0">An idea or piece of code which closely follows the most common idioms of the Python language, rather than implementing code using concepts common to other languages. For example, a common idiom in Python is to loop over all elements of an iterable using a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#for" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ec644571d9834e2dac71126fb999a60f"><span data-offset-key="ec644571d9834e2dac71126fb999a60f:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">for</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8d62a6a18c2d48e7a9c3706c7c1cacbf"><span data-offset-key="8d62a6a18c2d48e7a9c3706c7c1cacbf:0"> statement. Many other languages don’t have this type of construct, so people unfamiliar with Python sometimes use a numerical counter instead:</span></span></span>

    for i in range(len(food)):    print(food[i])

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="45e695f699534b9c91811be2951a1bb1"><span data-offset-key="45e695f699534b9c91811be2951a1bb1:0">As opposed to the cleaner, Pythonic method:</span></span></span>

    for piece in food:    print(piece)

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f207ca28eee24a19b848a87b304e2985"><span data-offset-key="f207ca28eee24a19b848a87b304e2985:0">qualified name</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="600204e8751f4e86b2f77114e9db81a7"><span data-offset-key="600204e8751f4e86b2f77114e9db81a7:0">A dotted name showing the “path” from a module’s global scope to a class, function or method defined in that module, as defined in </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-3155" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bfc73047a8784867b261f41642a45e70"><span data-offset-key="bfc73047a8784867b261f41642a45e70:0"><strong>PEP 3155</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="3b5c33b2ac744c5b84c020e6a6b89191"><span data-offset-key="3b5c33b2ac744c5b84c020e6a6b89191:0">. For top-level functions and classes, the qualified name is the same as the object’s name:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> class C:...     class D:...         def meth(self):...             pass...>>> C.__qualname__'C'>>> C.D.__qualname__'C.D'>>> C.D.meth.__qualname__'C.D.meth'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="00b8ee30f6b74905adaaa26662517d62"><span data-offset-key="00b8ee30f6b74905adaaa26662517d62:0">When used to refer to modules, the </span><span data-offset-key="00b8ee30f6b74905adaaa26662517d62:1">*fully qualified name*</span><span data-offset-key="00b8ee30f6b74905adaaa26662517d62:2"> means the entire dotted path to the module, including any parent packages, e.g. </span><span data-offset-key="00b8ee30f6b74905adaaa26662517d62:3">`email.mime.text`</span><span data-offset-key="00b8ee30f6b74905adaaa26662517d62:4">:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

    >>> import email.mime.text>>> email.mime.text.__name__'email.mime.text'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6ecbd95b206a4372970d910ca2805b23"><span data-offset-key="6ecbd95b206a4372970d910ca2805b23:0">reference count</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="823a2c01d83940fe950bbd6046e204af"><span data-offset-key="823a2c01d83940fe950bbd6046e204af:0">The number of references to an object. When the reference count of an object drops to zero, it is deallocated. Reference counting is generally not visible to Python code, but it is a key element of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-cpython" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="446226b726bb4fe8912e0f11a9f3ba5f"><span data-offset-key="446226b726bb4fe8912e0f11a9f3ba5f:0">CPython</span></span></a><span data-key="27b113ea82cf49819d7381bf2f8fb34f"><span data-offset-key="27b113ea82cf49819d7381bf2f8fb34f:0"> implementation. The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#module-sys" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3310348d3f6f494a8a57bba6dfd08500"><span data-offset-key="3310348d3f6f494a8a57bba6dfd08500:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c5352251a8554f2fb79b870c38c759f3"><span data-offset-key="c5352251a8554f2fb79b870c38c759f3:0"> module defines a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.getrefcount" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="30731c60ffe844c19d7b5896b2f7ec33"><span data-offset-key="30731c60ffe844c19d7b5896b2f7ec33:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">getrefcount()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="38cd6430a7ee45cfb8425c8d949a3c16"><span data-offset-key="38cd6430a7ee45cfb8425c8d949a3c16:0"> function that programmers can call to return the reference count for a particular object.regular package</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ca64517560454d12af59323a4644d0d4"><span data-offset-key="ca64517560454d12af59323a4644d0d4:0">A traditional </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ba913a3014934b0580540cf7bdd82e08"><span data-offset-key="ba913a3014934b0580540cf7bdd82e08:0">package</span></span></a><span data-key="d8c84f9a3c0847018338209393715e3e"><span data-offset-key="d8c84f9a3c0847018338209393715e3e:0">, such as a directory containing an </span><span data-offset-key="d8c84f9a3c0847018338209393715e3e:1">`__init__.py`</span><span data-offset-key="d8c84f9a3c0847018338209393715e3e:2"> file.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a868400122fe4f4697e41256fe74eebc"><span data-offset-key="a868400122fe4f4697e41256fe74eebc:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-namespace-package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4ea58530f148499ba8195656536e4c73"><span data-offset-key="4ea58530f148499ba8195656536e4c73:0">namespace package</span></span></a><span data-key="aa02537081be4c6e9c9a10d65cd9316c"><span data-offset-key="aa02537081be4c6e9c9a10d65cd9316c:0">.\_\_slots\_\_</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fc072f1578174e68a0099ce75e9d4e29"><span data-offset-key="fc072f1578174e68a0099ce75e9d4e29:0">A declaration inside a class that saves memory by pre-declaring space for instance attributes and eliminating instance dictionaries. Though popular, the technique is somewhat tricky to get right and is best reserved for rare cases where there are large numbers of instances in a memory-critical application.sequence</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b553d53478e4ad980d5c06b5ebb2215"><span data-offset-key="9b553d53478e4ad980d5c06b5ebb2215:0">An </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="571143185fbc4259b9bead5373e07faa"><span data-offset-key="571143185fbc4259b9bead5373e07faa:0">iterable</span></span></a><span data-key="3ec324bcd4534c55863af03ae9507922"><span data-offset-key="3ec324bcd4534c55863af03ae9507922:0"> which supports efficient element access using integer indices via the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="797cd0efdf5c458f80789650604b8f16"><span data-offset-key="797cd0efdf5c458f80789650604b8f16:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="5c648f5b2a12472f84ab68abede58ad9"><span data-offset-key="5c648f5b2a12472f84ab68abede58ad9:0"> special method and defines a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__len__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="837d359c8b524df68c0c05aeb1784b63"><span data-offset-key="837d359c8b524df68c0c05aeb1784b63:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__len__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="df3a45ed36e348aab0cd800cd9203072"><span data-offset-key="df3a45ed36e348aab0cd800cd9203072:0"> method that returns the length of the sequence. Some built-in sequence types are </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b372936e68cf4f13a44028962d949899"><span data-offset-key="b372936e68cf4f13a44028962d949899:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">list</code></span></span></a><span data-key="6398fb04db214669b531143dd443122e"><span data-offset-key="6398fb04db214669b531143dd443122e:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="68bd0eebd0774f0ab01b29c9616b806d"><span data-offset-key="68bd0eebd0774f0ab01b29c9616b806d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="595fd7b205654cb2b325c507ab9b9e57"><span data-offset-key="595fd7b205654cb2b325c507ab9b9e57:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ccfb62cacb194652baf3c69f06bdf34e"><span data-offset-key="ccfb62cacb194652baf3c69f06bdf34e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">tuple</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8a0a4237dac449e1937c2dda573c3373"><span data-offset-key="8a0a4237dac449e1937c2dda573c3373:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4821138c98d54a5aacd3c076ec136559"><span data-offset-key="4821138c98d54a5aacd3c076ec136559:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e6418b299f6445fc85ff044b99496a89"><span data-offset-key="e6418b299f6445fc85ff044b99496a89:0">. Note that </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="382b60cceaa04612816080c76b6c7c86"><span data-offset-key="382b60cceaa04612816080c76b6c7c86:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">dict</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f574164b9c484b9b90ecee45373f4dbc"><span data-offset-key="f574164b9c484b9b90ecee45373f4dbc:0"> also supports </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c2a6923fd210403081242973d662a41e"><span data-offset-key="c2a6923fd210403081242973d662a41e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ee18692a17aa4fe7b1ad22c5aca9b7fa"><span data-offset-key="ee18692a17aa4fe7b1ad22c5aca9b7fa:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__len__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="39146d009535440283a43899b9855564"><span data-offset-key="39146d009535440283a43899b9855564:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__len__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f6b3bbe6e0e845ceba6f2969a4504767"><span data-offset-key="f6b3bbe6e0e845ceba6f2969a4504767:0">, but is considered a mapping rather than a sequence because the lookups use arbitrary </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-immutable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="18a4de182e704b038f23de770f7b5cdb"><span data-offset-key="18a4de182e704b038f23de770f7b5cdb:0">immutable</span></span></a><span data-key="1bf01884f8ab490e8b4638a311e8a2f4"><span data-offset-key="1bf01884f8ab490e8b4638a311e8a2f4:0"> keys rather than integers.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4a54b7e368ee4e1a9d478ea59f4bc544"><span data-offset-key="4a54b7e368ee4e1a9d478ea59f4bc544:0">The </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.abc.html#collections.abc.Sequence" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e4d23ec6b558425eaca6facddedaddb5"><span data-offset-key="e4d23ec6b558425eaca6facddedaddb5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">collections.abc.Sequence</code></span></span></a><span data-key="07f1aa982de94ef1bb09bd943ac9a880"><span data-offset-key="07f1aa982de94ef1bb09bd943ac9a880:0"> abstract base class defines a much richer interface that goes beyond just </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fce539b20060458088c5f42570f8cd85"><span data-offset-key="fce539b20060458088c5f42570f8cd85:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__getitem__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="415c84bfe10245399889a4ef1176c757"><span data-offset-key="415c84bfe10245399889a4ef1176c757:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__len__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="604090ed6b554f3dacd0d24f33e55e37"><span data-offset-key="604090ed6b554f3dacd0d24f33e55e37:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__len__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="e6f765463a62445d9f2c1b0ee5b96c8d"><span data-offset-key="e6f765463a62445d9f2c1b0ee5b96c8d:0">, adding </span><span data-offset-key="e6f765463a62445d9f2c1b0ee5b96c8d:1">`count()`</span><span data-offset-key="e6f765463a62445d9f2c1b0ee5b96c8d:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="e6f765463a62445d9f2c1b0ee5b96c8d:3">`index()`</span><span data-offset-key="e6f765463a62445d9f2c1b0ee5b96c8d:4">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__contains__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2f06c14d94574d9ab50c1560a1a72e44"><span data-offset-key="2f06c14d94574d9ab50c1560a1a72e44:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__contains__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="82801373304c45beacd2fea3e9a5717c"><span data-offset-key="82801373304c45beacd2fea3e9a5717c:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__reversed__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="69eab0921fda4d1f8ce389635b1c8c48"><span data-offset-key="69eab0921fda4d1f8ce389635b1c8c48:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__reversed__()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="68673007def64ca6ad399e3067a5a503"><span data-offset-key="68673007def64ca6ad399e3067a5a503:0">. Types that implement this expanded interface can be registered explicitly using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/abc.html#abc.ABCMeta.register" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="950f825e590e43389bde63e936a1d08c"><span data-offset-key="950f825e590e43389bde63e936a1d08c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">register()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8de4b588b4f243879b46ac40382b7adf"><span data-offset-key="8de4b588b4f243879b46ac40382b7adf:0">.set comprehension</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="99814bad13ab494a8d75c24f73f0bb2a"><span data-offset-key="99814bad13ab494a8d75c24f73f0bb2a:0">A compact way to process all or part of the elements in an iterable and return a set with the results. </span><span data-offset-key="99814bad13ab494a8d75c24f73f0bb2a:1">`results = {c for c in                                       'abracadabra' if c not in                                       'abc'}`</span><span data-offset-key="99814bad13ab494a8d75c24f73f0bb2a:2"> generates the set of strings </span><span data-offset-key="99814bad13ab494a8d75c24f73f0bb2a:3">`{'r', 'd'}`</span><span data-offset-key="99814bad13ab494a8d75c24f73f0bb2a:4">. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#comprehensions" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="070284e399334f67b0d7ad9ccbac7e04"><span data-offset-key="070284e399334f67b0d7ad9ccbac7e04:0">Displays for lists, sets and dictionaries</span></span></a><span data-key="594f6ca4a747469b837d6e1fc2a4554a"><span data-offset-key="594f6ca4a747469b837d6e1fc2a4554a:0">.single dispatch</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="123051ad80b443aca9c2987ef1bc945c"><span data-offset-key="123051ad80b443aca9c2987ef1bc945c:0">A form of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-generic-function" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="148493f8b6b64a6f9db3116b96f8bd9a"><span data-offset-key="148493f8b6b64a6f9db3116b96f8bd9a:0">generic function</span></span></a><span data-key="9e7fb5b58cef481cbaa45874b97ac72b"><span data-offset-key="9e7fb5b58cef481cbaa45874b97ac72b:0"> dispatch where the implementation is chosen based on the type of a single argument.slice</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cc33cb9a1e0f4252a04acdbe3c050e60"><span data-offset-key="cc33cb9a1e0f4252a04acdbe3c050e60:0">An object usually containing a portion of a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-sequence" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4867e1ededc24eb6871f66bdccdfa9bb"><span data-offset-key="4867e1ededc24eb6871f66bdccdfa9bb:0">sequence</span></span></a><span data-key="34f368d310be44299684350b41d18069"><span data-offset-key="34f368d310be44299684350b41d18069:0">. A slice is created using the subscript notation, </span><span data-offset-key="34f368d310be44299684350b41d18069:1">`[]`</span><span data-offset-key="34f368d310be44299684350b41d18069:2"> with colons between numbers when several are given, such as in </span><span data-offset-key="34f368d310be44299684350b41d18069:3">`variable_name[1:3:5]`</span><span data-offset-key="34f368d310be44299684350b41d18069:4">. The bracket (subscript) notation uses </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#slice" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="000139a991ae4254a2352c49fbdbd0a0"><span data-offset-key="000139a991ae4254a2352c49fbdbd0a0:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">slice</code></span></span></a><span data-key="9dd138e75fdc4d49aa2c0e96ab9259f6"><span data-offset-key="9dd138e75fdc4d49aa2c0e96ab9259f6:0"> objects internally.special method</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="601e501580ba42b68aeb244127e211d1"><span data-offset-key="601e501580ba42b68aeb244127e211d1:0">A method that is called implicitly by Python to execute a certain operation on a type, such as addition. Such methods have names starting and ending with double underscores. Special methods are documented in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#specialnames" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2c856587d74f4d108b3c28b413fe21e8"><span data-offset-key="2c856587d74f4d108b3c28b413fe21e8:0">Special method names</span></span></a><span data-key="3ac3fdee65f546ee9e46c5f5b2b006bc"><span data-offset-key="3ac3fdee65f546ee9e46c5f5b2b006bc:0">.statement</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f3e0800018894b76a651e4d1d3e61be4"><span data-offset-key="f3e0800018894b76a651e4d1d3e61be4:0">A statement is part of a suite (a “block” of code).
