A statement is either an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-expression" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7222e0063a404d03b8a43a44820e9931"><span data-offset-key="7222e0063a404d03b8a43a44820e9931:0">expression</span></span></a><span data-key="3863213bd5eb4b59bc24a2920073d7ab"><span data-offset-key="3863213bd5eb4b59bc24a2920073d7ab:0"> or one of several constructs with a keyword, such as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#if" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ad09c485aec640c7a214697d882446d8"><span data-offset-key="ad09c485aec640c7a214697d882446d8:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">if</code></span></span></a><span data-key="c0fafa2ad0064363a367ad749c1e726c"><span data-offset-key="c0fafa2ad0064363a367ad749c1e726c:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#while" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2f71517978cc40e78720c92bcf824992"><span data-offset-key="2f71517978cc40e78720c92bcf824992:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">while</code></span></span></a><span data-key="782de5855d484b529c156de8e963a3e4"><span data-offset-key="782de5855d484b529c156de8e963a3e4:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/compound_stmts.html#for" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fbfff3997d4a40718d3858e89d55c50d"><span data-offset-key="fbfff3997d4a40718d3858e89d55c50d:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">for</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0c52b4f2666b4d4397c3775bade28f10"><span data-offset-key="0c52b4f2666b4d4397c3775bade28f10:0">.text encoding</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a886565e52114e6683519d4b27cfa9ff"><span data-offset-key="a886565e52114e6683519d4b27cfa9ff:0">A codec which encodes Unicode strings to bytes.text file</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2f5180f984db44f499a0ab8d892c1a58"><span data-offset-key="2f5180f984db44f499a0ab8d892c1a58:0">A </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-file-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c3384ef349bb4324b9b765e18cc966a7"><span data-offset-key="c3384ef349bb4324b9b765e18cc966a7:0">file object</span></span></a><span data-key="0e8132268f7c433e8201f0161d7a1108"><span data-offset-key="0e8132268f7c433e8201f0161d7a1108:0"> able to read and write </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e468cae2eb144808bb91695d824926e7"><span data-offset-key="e468cae2eb144808bb91695d824926e7:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">str</code></span></span></a><span data-key="b6821f3978354c00bcc6c6da75902688"><span data-offset-key="b6821f3978354c00bcc6c6da75902688:0"> objects. Often, a text file actually accesses a byte-oriented data stream and handles the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-text-encoding" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4b6c7c517f4c4c29a63c92331fb63b3e"><span data-offset-key="4b6c7c517f4c4c29a63c92331fb63b3e:0">text encoding</span></span></a><span data-key="46d8ede44b074b4eb6a207188045260f"><span data-offset-key="46d8ede44b074b4eb6a207188045260f:0"> automatically. Examples of text files are files opened in text mode (</span><span data-offset-key="46d8ede44b074b4eb6a207188045260f:1">`'r'`</span><span data-offset-key="46d8ede44b074b4eb6a207188045260f:2"> or </span><span data-offset-key="46d8ede44b074b4eb6a207188045260f:3">`'w'`</span><span data-offset-key="46d8ede44b074b4eb6a207188045260f:4">), </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.stdin" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b50f6c994bb74356a7186c519886f566"><span data-offset-key="b50f6c994bb74356a7186c519886f566:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.stdin</code></span></span></a><span data-key="ba9250492a8d4825963da7234e2836fa"><span data-offset-key="ba9250492a8d4825963da7234e2836fa:0">, </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.stdout" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dc7f9898f306404b91cee9f1790e2c50"><span data-offset-key="dc7f9898f306404b91cee9f1790e2c50:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.stdout</code></span></span></a><span data-key="904103842e9c44b79edccab029aeee83"><span data-offset-key="904103842e9c44b79edccab029aeee83:0">, and instances of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.StringIO" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="31ee816e8c7349de91d2c0530f285642"><span data-offset-key="31ee816e8c7349de91d2c0530f285642:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">io.StringIO</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0680d1b7c8fc4895a35a3c75b304d536"><span data-offset-key="0680d1b7c8fc4895a35a3c75b304d536:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b1895fbe727d40f0b0f7eef7e0de506e"><span data-offset-key="b1895fbe727d40f0b0f7eef7e0de506e:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-binary-file" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9e52a0b6cc654d0fa090e95d6f5bfe20"><span data-offset-key="9e52a0b6cc654d0fa090e95d6f5bfe20:0">binary file</span></span></a><span data-key="eef898371b574c1bb686db25e9257b66"><span data-offset-key="eef898371b574c1bb686db25e9257b66:0"> for a file object able to read and write </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytes-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e10f398241af4a139d8732a03ffdf33a"><span data-offset-key="e10f398241af4a139d8732a03ffdf33a:0">bytes-like objects</span></span></a><span data-key="5ba94b2b5f6b472e9022c1208eaeb6db"><span data-offset-key="5ba94b2b5f6b472e9022c1208eaeb6db:0">.triple-quoted string</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11672609fe1f4a578c9973d0d5745df8"><span data-offset-key="11672609fe1f4a578c9973d0d5745df8:0">A string which is bound by three instances of either a quotation mark (“) or an apostrophe (‘). While they don’t provide any functionality not available with single-quoted strings, they are useful for a number of reasons. They allow you to include unescaped single and double quotes within a string and they can span multiple lines without the use of the continuation character, making them especially useful when writing docstrings.type</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="07d00e5189d6416eb83f5b97f6413893"><span data-offset-key="07d00e5189d6416eb83f5b97f6413893:0">The type of a Python object determines what kind of object it is; every object has a type. An object’s type is accessible as its </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#instance.__class__" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ccb5a544b5ff4ff39674d49eec75e09e"><span data-offset-key="ccb5a544b5ff4ff39674d49eec75e09e:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">__class__</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8a55699941384b5489117199a9f207b2"><span data-offset-key="8a55699941384b5489117199a9f207b2:0"> attribute or can be retrieved with </span><span data-offset-key="8a55699941384b5489117199a9f207b2:1">`type(obj)`</span><span data-offset-key="8a55699941384b5489117199a9f207b2:2">.type alias</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6f105f65894a45c8981a2033a2f767ab"><span data-offset-key="6f105f65894a45c8981a2033a2f767ab:0">A synonym for a type, created by assigning the type to an identifier.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6df8c10ce3ca480b9cec70e8c8f16696"><span data-offset-key="6df8c10ce3ca480b9cec70e8c8f16696:0">Type aliases are useful for simplifying </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-type-hint" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="13dac84e0b6341d6b2792d837f8656cc"><span data-offset-key="13dac84e0b6341d6b2792d837f8656cc:0">type hints</span></span></a><span data-key="055552a6c6a8410fa35ec13aba352523"><span data-offset-key="055552a6c6a8410fa35ec13aba352523:0">. For example:</span></span></span>

    def remove_gray_shades(        colors: list[tuple[int, int, int]]) -> list[tuple[int, int, int]]:    pass

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bb4d875806c448238747971c2761e5c4"><span data-offset-key="bb4d875806c448238747971c2761e5c4:0">could be made more readable like this:</span></span></span>

    Color = tuple[int, int, int]​def remove_gray_shades(colors: list[Color]) -> list[Color]:    pass

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="06f6136e0b484e6ea96c3698af83871d"><span data-offset-key="06f6136e0b484e6ea96c3698af83871d:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/typing.html#module-typing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9275fc4ae447483b8f661c4d39e04db3"><span data-offset-key="9275fc4ae447483b8f661c4d39e04db3:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">typing</code></span></span></a><span data-key="8d3564861532443183478b9dec5141ed"><span data-offset-key="8d3564861532443183478b9dec5141ed:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0484" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="778bea9fd0af4647a32f7ea9edb3c737"><span data-offset-key="778bea9fd0af4647a32f7ea9edb3c737:0"><strong>PEP 484</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="ce90c55c330c4cd09cfc0983e3fdb095"><span data-offset-key="ce90c55c330c4cd09cfc0983e3fdb095:0">, which describe this functionality.type hint</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="55f4039c0395495cb136bd445cb33c16"><span data-offset-key="55f4039c0395495cb136bd445cb33c16:0">An </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-annotation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3b1135a5e5e745339129c93decb71317"><span data-offset-key="3b1135a5e5e745339129c93decb71317:0">annotation</span></span></a><span data-key="1b5f7fd0b4174e9a8001e613d52f9e16"><span data-offset-key="1b5f7fd0b4174e9a8001e613d52f9e16:0"> that specifies the expected type for a variable, a class attribute, or a function parameter or return value.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fe6bf60a496d4796a8994dc2722be3d7"><span data-offset-key="fe6bf60a496d4796a8994dc2722be3d7:0">Type hints are optional and are not enforced by Python but they are useful to static type analysis tools, and aid IDEs with code completion and refactoring.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b96c228aabaa4353bf07c2c3f43ddd7f"><span data-offset-key="b96c228aabaa4353bf07c2c3f43ddd7f:0">Type hints of global variables, class attributes, and functions, but not local variables, can be accessed using </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/typing.html#typing.get_type_hints" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="53568cc9be64464f8f481f2bd37e9cae"><span data-offset-key="53568cc9be64464f8f481f2bd37e9cae:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">typing.get_type_hints()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="f31a88fe279c4be0b53fcffc471a5c74"><span data-offset-key="f31a88fe279c4be0b53fcffc471a5c74:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b9630cf1c7184096aa0d856843184a74"><span data-offset-key="b9630cf1c7184096aa0d856843184a74:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/typing.html#module-typing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8139652f74bd43e58b5663051e7ee685"><span data-offset-key="8139652f74bd43e58b5663051e7ee685:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">typing</code></span></span></a><span data-key="a123df7194494b8fb58bb0636c5eefcc"><span data-offset-key="a123df7194494b8fb58bb0636c5eefcc:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0484" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="895c5504811b49fc9470427bbe4f35e7"><span data-offset-key="895c5504811b49fc9470427bbe4f35e7:0"><strong>PEP 484</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="fe3e5a87ac1f44a5a0211bb4840bad99"><span data-offset-key="fe3e5a87ac1f44a5a0211bb4840bad99:0">, which describe this functionality.universal newlines</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="81bfc14bd1d947db8f73e51a7de7c301"><span data-offset-key="81bfc14bd1d947db8f73e51a7de7c301:0">A manner of interpreting text streams in which all of the following are recognized as ending a line: the Unix end-of-line convention </span><span data-offset-key="81bfc14bd1d947db8f73e51a7de7c301:1">`'\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="81bfc14bd1d947db8f73e51a7de7c301:2">, the Windows convention </span><span data-offset-key="81bfc14bd1d947db8f73e51a7de7c301:3">`'\r\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="81bfc14bd1d947db8f73e51a7de7c301:4">, and the old Macintosh convention </span><span data-offset-key="81bfc14bd1d947db8f73e51a7de7c301:5">`'\r'`</span><span data-offset-key="81bfc14bd1d947db8f73e51a7de7c301:6">. See </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0278" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="74cf325ba9a140658f5c425fa624179e"><span data-offset-key="74cf325ba9a140658f5c425fa624179e:0"><strong>PEP 278</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="50383a49ac4e43409c1864b77264a44c"><span data-offset-key="50383a49ac4e43409c1864b77264a44c:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-3116" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="51a27afc94ff4df18f0dc2b91c68ed8a"><span data-offset-key="51a27afc94ff4df18f0dc2b91c68ed8a:0"><strong>PEP 3116</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="66eb6b3e4e694596b47fa9e516783597"><span data-offset-key="66eb6b3e4e694596b47fa9e516783597:0">, as well as </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes.splitlines" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dc690b8f3756418ead515c8fc28d0778"><span data-offset-key="dc690b8f3756418ead515c8fc28d0778:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">bytes.splitlines()</code></span></span></a><span data-key="0d0d615716a74fd4b3e59d191e3f62c8"><span data-offset-key="0d0d615716a74fd4b3e59d191e3f62c8:0"> for an additional use.variable annotation</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c9173caf8f7146bea3b9031b4c717608"><span data-offset-key="c9173caf8f7146bea3b9031b4c717608:0">An </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-annotation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="37b0fa58ce87450187d97da77e9393d1"><span data-offset-key="37b0fa58ce87450187d97da77e9393d1:0">annotation</span></span></a><span data-key="83381671d1b74c0b93f1998a7be1eac0"><span data-offset-key="83381671d1b74c0b93f1998a7be1eac0:0"> of a variable or a class attribute.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e112d0d591384cd88b315cb3fdf43ea7"><span data-offset-key="e112d0d591384cd88b315cb3fdf43ea7:0">When annotating a variable or a class attribute, assignment is optional:</span></span></span>

    class C:    field: 'annotation'

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cf921eb447734c1e8f53ac208e2995df"><span data-offset-key="cf921eb447734c1e8f53ac208e2995df:0">Variable annotations are usually used for </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-type-hint" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1626410c27f2495889080d196ac87f33"><span data-offset-key="1626410c27f2495889080d196ac87f33:0">type hints</span></span></a><span data-key="98178b9377c64f589cf6028296097a54"><span data-offset-key="98178b9377c64f589cf6028296097a54:0">: for example this variable is expected to take </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7abfab57d5164e10a908503be7d0e41c"><span data-offset-key="7abfab57d5164e10a908503be7d0e41c:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">int</code></span></span></a><span data-key="50ca03269f9f4089ab94b98f51a23bbf"><span data-offset-key="50ca03269f9f4089ab94b98f51a23bbf:0"> values:</span></span></span>

    count: int = 0

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="32fe5b702cc449f9917c3829e6f5d6bb"><span data-offset-key="32fe5b702cc449f9917c3829e6f5d6bb:0">Variable annotation syntax is explained in section </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/simple_stmts.html#annassign" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6f9a5f3127e640e3aa54d787ad46471c"><span data-offset-key="6f9a5f3127e640e3aa54d787ad46471c:0">Annotated assignment statements</span></span></a><span data-key="25f87cbf3dbe4effa79495d4ce3287a7"><span data-offset-key="25f87cbf3dbe4effa79495d4ce3287a7:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="698e4def49b145a29e83ab72baf1eb65"><span data-offset-key="698e4def49b145a29e83ab72baf1eb65:0">See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-function-annotation" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="823613bf7d8d48a1a5354042fe3d1da0"><span data-offset-key="823613bf7d8d48a1a5354042fe3d1da0:0">function annotation</span></span></a><span data-key="d0153d1397114014b6e9c69f7f34e738"><span data-offset-key="d0153d1397114014b6e9c69f7f34e738:0">, </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0484" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d73cb85e1d244d36b1888e84297c26a6"><span data-offset-key="d73cb85e1d244d36b1888e84297c26a6:0"><strong>PEP 484</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="970c65b8df374f5cbcbd64f9012e03c1"><span data-offset-key="970c65b8df374f5cbcbd64f9012e03c1:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0526" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="367792a0579147c8b993ffb24120776c"><span data-offset-key="367792a0579147c8b993ffb24120776c:0"><strong>PEP 526</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="fd23078ad54f47908e2eb6b28be68259"><span data-offset-key="fd23078ad54f47908e2eb6b28be68259:0">, which describe this functionality.virtual environment</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f4ed9722a80249b79af5892707fbbc73"><span data-offset-key="f4ed9722a80249b79af5892707fbbc73:0">A cooperatively isolated runtime environment that allows Python users and applications to install and upgrade Python distribution packages without interfering with the behaviour of other Python applications running on the same system.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="82721eb22eac411ba4d02c9a84e4f0f4"><span data-offset-key="82721eb22eac411ba4d02c9a84e4f0f4:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/venv.html#module-venv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e03d08ed105648859dba8dbe5a43e6fe"><span data-offset-key="e03d08ed105648859dba8dbe5a43e6fe:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">venv</code></span></span></a><span data-key="7c15777a22ec44649190dfef75f4ee77"><span data-offset-key="7c15777a22ec44649190dfef75f4ee77:0">.virtual machine</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6aaeeed3377c46d988d2285a52b6288e"><span data-offset-key="6aaeeed3377c46d988d2285a52b6288e:0">A computer defined entirely in software. Python’s virtual machine executes the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-bytecode" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1ba1bd614a554bb6a961e053718c1dd6"><span data-offset-key="1ba1bd614a554bb6a961e053718c1dd6:0">bytecode</span></span></a><span data-key="e5d9928953b0449f8f4e0a2c2c41bc8c"><span data-offset-key="e5d9928953b0449f8f4e0a2c2c41bc8c:0"> emitted by the bytecode compiler.Zen of Python</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ded2bdfde12545299840eee65a6e6812"><span data-offset-key="ded2bdfde12545299840eee65a6e6812:0">Listing of Python design principles and philosophies that are helpful in understanding and using the language. The listing can be found by typing “</span><span data-offset-key="ded2bdfde12545299840eee65a6e6812:1">`import this`</span><span data-offset-key="ded2bdfde12545299840eee65a6e6812:2">” at the interactive prompt.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="81892bb6935d4c7ba04164cad1b8e576"><span data-offset-key="81892bb6935d4c7ba04164cad1b8e576:0">**Binary Distribution**</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d2f402418e154028adfe86053c96227f"><span data-offset-key="d2f402418e154028adfe86053c96227f:0">A specific kind of </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Built-Distribution" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c8aa9a911f8f429d9d92f7ebdbeef01e"><span data-offset-key="c8aa9a911f8f429d9d92f7ebdbeef01e:0">Built Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="1749eb38dca843aaa2d8d0df7eb938ff"><span data-offset-key="1749eb38dca843aaa2d8d0df7eb938ff:0"> that contains compiled extensions.Built Distribution</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="705d261823b74fb9a205e337aa2ab4cf"><span data-offset-key="705d261823b74fb9a205e337aa2ab4cf:0">A </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="15039209b2e048169527b459a9278781"><span data-offset-key="15039209b2e048169527b459a9278781:0">Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="77266cefd4494c76acc65e00f7d8f684"><span data-offset-key="77266cefd4494c76acc65e00f7d8f684:0"> format containing files and metadata that only need to be moved to the correct location on the target system, to be installed. </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Wheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="35a7ccdf82a749df987640bf37747e14"><span data-offset-key="35a7ccdf82a749df987640bf37747e14:0">Wheel</span></span></a><span data-key="46cf4c1466d74cec8eaa0b3871ccb781"><span data-offset-key="46cf4c1466d74cec8eaa0b3871ccb781:0"> is such a format, whereas distutil’s </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Source-Distribution-or-sdist" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f60b6f905ee94ff2b4cd06e6f77c575c"><span data-offset-key="f60b6f905ee94ff2b4cd06e6f77c575c:0">Source Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="48a4915c132e44758eed5704f87b10dc"><span data-offset-key="48a4915c132e44758eed5704f87b10dc:0"> is not, in that it requires a build step before it can be installed. This format does not imply that Python files have to be precompiled (</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Wheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bbad18f3c63540b3a16bb01bcb5b3002"><span data-offset-key="bbad18f3c63540b3a16bb01bcb5b3002:0">Wheel</span></span></a><span data-key="f07b92bce0204666999efc157100ff26"><span data-offset-key="f07b92bce0204666999efc157100ff26:0"> intentionally does not include compiled Python files).Distribution Package</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ec5d50e2176846df83754fa040c58b02"><span data-offset-key="ec5d50e2176846df83754fa040c58b02:0">A versioned archive file that contains Python </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Import-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="75a280961da14859b6abbaa405e0f718"><span data-offset-key="75a280961da14859b6abbaa405e0f718:0">packages</span></span></a><span data-key="3595f91cca9047f199922bc6096393ba"><span data-offset-key="3595f91cca9047f199922bc6096393ba:0">, </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="970c35c9de2941c5807c4a8db1995c15"><span data-offset-key="970c35c9de2941c5807c4a8db1995c15:0">modules</span></span></a><span data-key="570b8b57df38490bba9d0983d7322cd7"><span data-offset-key="570b8b57df38490bba9d0983d7322cd7:0">, and other resource files that are used to distribute a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Release" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a477b38f2fd0495eb70722f7185a6a7c"><span data-offset-key="a477b38f2fd0495eb70722f7185a6a7c:0">Release</span></span></a><span data-key="680fa92f188f49719acac5ffe33edd53"><span data-offset-key="680fa92f188f49719acac5ffe33edd53:0">. The archive file is what an end-user will download from the internet and install.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="929334f5cab04bb39e6e863a105b6db0"><span data-offset-key="929334f5cab04bb39e6e863a105b6db0:0">A distribution package is more commonly referred to with the single words “package” or “distribution”, but this guide may use the expanded term when more clarity is needed to prevent confusion with an </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Import-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b663c018e3cc41e1abf683c3aa35fc74"><span data-offset-key="b663c018e3cc41e1abf683c3aa35fc74:0">Import Package</span></span></a><span data-key="626f17a677b54abf8623504d87b081eb"><span data-offset-key="626f17a677b54abf8623504d87b081eb:0"> (which is also commonly called a “package”) or another kind of distribution (e.g. a Linux distribution or the Python language distribution), which are often referred to with the single term “distribution”.Egg</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11357d9742774aeaba987b8e48a85fdd"><span data-offset-key="11357d9742774aeaba987b8e48a85fdd:0">A </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Built-Distribution" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="789a170f37ca4846afdeecb2515a9a53"><span data-offset-key="789a170f37ca4846afdeecb2515a9a53:0">Built Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="2771892d5e944eb2a02c09b0c0029b4e"><span data-offset-key="2771892d5e944eb2a02c09b0c0029b4e:0"> format introduced by </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="353a22b724d54ecea97b5ce31f9f19c8"><span data-offset-key="353a22b724d54ecea97b5ce31f9f19c8:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="941aeba0e4a04a95becb892722c0d8ab"><span data-offset-key="941aeba0e4a04a95becb892722c0d8ab:0">, which is being replaced by </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Wheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1146f85e5df1407a91ab2deb497dfc80"><span data-offset-key="1146f85e5df1407a91ab2deb497dfc80:0">Wheel</span></span></a><span data-key="2bc77221d7c44f0482e768d42347cff3"><span data-offset-key="2bc77221d7c44f0482e768d42347cff3:0">. For details, see \` </span></span><a href="https://setuptools.readthedocs.io/en/latest/deprecated/python_eggs.html" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bdbaa37810c346209e2caaf2eb7b9db2"><span data-offset-key="bdbaa37810c346209e2caaf2eb7b9db2:0">The Internal Structure of Python Eggs</span></span></a><span data-key="fbd6b1f8566e495f84f03bf27f7bc054"><span data-offset-key="fbd6b1f8566e495f84f03bf27f7bc054:0"> and </span></span><a href="http://peak.telecommunity.com/DevCenter/PythonEggs" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="71f6b6d09cba45f1831a9e0aa3b8127a"><span data-offset-key="71f6b6d09cba45f1831a9e0aa3b8127a:0">Python Eggs</span></span></a><span data-key="cc776d2221054e48927beb28c8f06658"><span data-offset-key="cc776d2221054e48927beb28c8f06658:0">Extension Module</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4459c1cde5db44798a360dd512261a72"><span data-offset-key="4459c1cde5db44798a360dd512261a72:0">A </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ea33e4ecf3a6440ea309669c4ccc496d"><span data-offset-key="ea33e4ecf3a6440ea309669c4ccc496d:0">Module</span></span></a><span data-key="c7f2b97f8bd04eff9f25e584c12422dc"><span data-offset-key="c7f2b97f8bd04eff9f25e584c12422dc:0"> written in the low-level language of the Python implementation: C/C++ for Python, Java for Jython. Typically contained in a single dynamically loadable pre-compiled file, e.g. a shared object (.so) file for Python extensions on Unix, a DLL (given the .pyd extension) for Python extensions on Windows, or a Java class file for Jython extensions.Known Good Set (KGS)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c20c226f77474212870f387798caac0b"><span data-offset-key="c20c226f77474212870f387798caac0b:0">A set of distributions at specified versions which are compatible with each other. Typically a test suite will be run which passes all tests before a specific set of packages is declared a known good set. This term is commonly used by frameworks and toolkits which are comprised of multiple individual distributions.Import Package</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="503116508c934ff2a89d1a0b9e9a8f47"><span data-offset-key="503116508c934ff2a89d1a0b9e9a8f47:0">A </span><span data-offset-key="503116508c934ff2a89d1a0b9e9a8f47:1">**Python module**</span><span data-offset-key="503116508c934ff2a89d1a0b9e9a8f47:2"> which can contain other modules or recursively, other packages.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b68c062d563847c9bad9e5bad68514d0"><span data-offset-key="b68c062d563847c9bad9e5bad68514d0:0">**An import package**</span><span data-offset-key="b68c062d563847c9bad9e5bad68514d0:1"> is more commonly referred to with the single word “package”, but this guide will use the expanded term when more clarity is needed to prevent confusion with a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e6799b649d114af3a6025c34f122429f"><span data-offset-key="e6799b649d114af3a6025c34f122429f:0">Distribution Package</span></span></a><span data-key="f451d5be97e94372b644d7422fb3b0e2"><span data-offset-key="f451d5be97e94372b644d7422fb3b0e2:0"> which is also commonly called a “package”.Module</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ca901c74d4414192826efb55898d6130"><span data-offset-key="ca901c74d4414192826efb55898d6130:0">The basic unit of code reusability in Python, existing in one of two types: </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Pure-Module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="40a9ef50fb9d4b39a40dd43c6b711e7b"><span data-offset-key="40a9ef50fb9d4b39a40dd43c6b711e7b:0">Pure Module</span></span></a><span data-key="9e6f77ebdea54d6b9913c94a448b2b7c"><span data-offset-key="9e6f77ebdea54d6b9913c94a448b2b7c:0">, or </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Extension-Module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="910a93ea0f0a4509bfc78fb535cf26dd"><span data-offset-key="910a93ea0f0a4509bfc78fb535cf26dd:0">Extension Module</span></span></a><span data-key="7c6936c97eb84c48bb4e28fc19d90add"><span data-offset-key="7c6936c97eb84c48bb4e28fc19d90add:0">.Package Index</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1bfc14dca3484c72b3d07de8a67c6e34"><span data-offset-key="1bfc14dca3484c72b3d07de8a67c6e34:0">A repository of distributions with a web interface to automate </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bbb42087377d44f4a6e03b11f78f2608"><span data-offset-key="bbb42087377d44f4a6e03b11f78f2608:0">package</span></span></a><span data-key="aedc3d569f2745bbbb2408fb1eb76c26"><span data-offset-key="aedc3d569f2745bbbb2408fb1eb76c26:0"> discovery and consumption.Per Project Index</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b35f8c550ecc4c5691f20b07b042ca19"><span data-offset-key="b35f8c550ecc4c5691f20b07b042ca19:0">A private or other non-canonical </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Package-Index" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0c1faa81e8654ae3b61797e49d126a06"><span data-offset-key="0c1faa81e8654ae3b61797e49d126a06:0">Package Index</span></span></a><span data-key="084b3337aee24889928763d613b3ed95"><span data-offset-key="084b3337aee24889928763d613b3ed95:0"> indicated by a specific </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Project" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2828d6ab95014e5889872e112b5a3416"><span data-offset-key="2828d6ab95014e5889872e112b5a3416:0">Project</span></span></a><span data-key="7542cc6429f54c80935fea99ea07a9ca"><span data-offset-key="7542cc6429f54c80935fea99ea07a9ca:0"> as the index preferred or required to resolve dependencies of that project.Project</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="809bbef1386c4cbcb584da677ec8fde0"><span data-offset-key="809bbef1386c4cbcb584da677ec8fde0:0">A library, framework, script, plugin, application, or collection of data or other resources, or some combination thereof that is intended to be packaged into a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="30131a5a7dd64320b6446353f98a03b7"><span data-offset-key="30131a5a7dd64320b6446353f98a03b7:0">Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="8c91260edd3849b5a716066ef0cbf517"><span data-offset-key="8c91260edd3849b5a716066ef0cbf517:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0ea01fcd17f34ecfa92c601e1360f76b"><span data-offset-key="0ea01fcd17f34ecfa92c601e1360f76b:0">Since most projects create </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7dd105a03c7c4f8ab49c67382875ca60"><span data-offset-key="7dd105a03c7c4f8ab49c67382875ca60:0">Distributions</span></span></a><span data-key="583e80859ba84e5f87b4a9d4d54edfdd"><span data-offset-key="583e80859ba84e5f87b4a9d4d54edfdd:0"> using either </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0518" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4af7320294df4415b926d873b71f50c6"><span data-offset-key="4af7320294df4415b926d873b71f50c6:0"><strong>PEP 518</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="b57990f4803349c3ae2b2281fe2d2f1f"><span data-offset-key="b57990f4803349c3ae2b2281fe2d2f1f:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="b57990f4803349c3ae2b2281fe2d2f1f:1">`build-system`</span><span data-offset-key="b57990f4803349c3ae2b2281fe2d2f1f:2">, </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#distutils" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="db9224f504f24345b1b1192ab98d01a6"><span data-offset-key="db9224f504f24345b1b1192ab98d01a6:0">distutils</span></span></a><span data-key="9c6de509b4bf4d58b89642caa0bc233d"><span data-offset-key="9c6de509b4bf4d58b89642caa0bc233d:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a417efed1dc445fd95f7f510fcf60985"><span data-offset-key="a417efed1dc445fd95f7f510fcf60985:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="a4198b9503e04ad989b9b0e01be60a73"><span data-offset-key="a4198b9503e04ad989b9b0e01be60a73:0">, another practical way to define projects currently is something that contains a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-pyproject.toml" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="275bfd372cb048bf8b7131c564b571c8"><span data-offset-key="275bfd372cb048bf8b7131c564b571c8:0">pyproject.toml</span></span></a><span data-key="8209e913c1984a17aa926ec1c7ea8978"><span data-offset-key="8209e913c1984a17aa926ec1c7ea8978:0">, </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-setup.py" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bd67d85a612c4156a7ecf60123524aa0"><span data-offset-key="bd67d85a612c4156a7ecf60123524aa0:0">setup.py</span></span></a><span data-key="6d3ea7f52f064acca406cf98caafb21f"><span data-offset-key="6d3ea7f52f064acca406cf98caafb21f:0">, or </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-setup.cfg" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="21639a3dbebe493b8afe019fe784f9d3"><span data-offset-key="21639a3dbebe493b8afe019fe784f9d3:0">setup.cfg</span></span></a><span data-key="cef0b118e98041fdb9181866e5c57ab0"><span data-offset-key="cef0b118e98041fdb9181866e5c57ab0:0"> file at the root of the project source directory.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f9a36c95e0b3495aa468f66a78145990"><span data-offset-key="f9a36c95e0b3495aa468f66a78145990:0">Python projects must have unique names, which are registered on </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Python-Package-Index-PyPI" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2d79818422ac41cf98ee787f3648bf4b"><span data-offset-key="2d79818422ac41cf98ee787f3648bf4b:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="3a9f564e6cad44dd971a763727786460"><span data-offset-key="3a9f564e6cad44dd971a763727786460:0">. Each project will then contain one or more </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Release" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c57b6610badb4400b4bda6a86577437e"><span data-offset-key="c57b6610badb4400b4bda6a86577437e:0">Releases</span></span></a><span data-key="0512b275894a4263a9117e6862f15848"><span data-offset-key="0512b275894a4263a9117e6862f15848:0">, and each release may comprise one or more </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e8856459ed204c91bdd4b6e1a02ef736"><span data-offset-key="e8856459ed204c91bdd4b6e1a02ef736:0">distributions</span></span></a><span data-key="6630ac4ed52a4e7ab27bb2b9ca8bc515"><span data-offset-key="6630ac4ed52a4e7ab27bb2b9ca8bc515:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2e7a10583d9e4df2a12e1e201417c92e"><span data-offset-key="2e7a10583d9e4df2a12e1e201417c92e:0">Note that there is a strong convention to name a project after the name of the package that is imported to run that project. However, this doesn’t have to hold true. It’s possible to install a distribution from the project ‘foo’ and have it provide a package importable only as ‘bar’.Pure Module</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5d43c167d75f4fa9b1358299b3d24525"><span data-offset-key="5d43c167d75f4fa9b1358299b3d24525:0">A </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Module" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7963aaf4cb8d4e0782cc6ff90231e1ee"><span data-offset-key="7963aaf4cb8d4e0782cc6ff90231e1ee:0">Module</span></span></a><span data-key="97598ad784ad44f49c04ab3cf2e6740f"><span data-offset-key="97598ad784ad44f49c04ab3cf2e6740f:0"> written in Python and contained in a single </span><span data-offset-key="97598ad784ad44f49c04ab3cf2e6740f:1">`.py`</span><span data-offset-key="97598ad784ad44f49c04ab3cf2e6740f:2"> file (and possibly associated </span><span data-offset-key="97598ad784ad44f49c04ab3cf2e6740f:3">`.pyc`</span><span data-offset-key="97598ad784ad44f49c04ab3cf2e6740f:4"> and/or </span><span data-offset-key="97598ad784ad44f49c04ab3cf2e6740f:5">`.pyo`</span><span data-offset-key="97598ad784ad44f49c04ab3cf2e6740f:6"> files).Python Packaging Authority (PyPA)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d42487edd01346a184ce3587b3d4b81e"><span data-offset-key="d42487edd01346a184ce3587b3d4b81e:0">PyPA is a working group that maintains many of the relevant projects in Python packaging. They maintain a site at </span></span><a href="https://www.pypa.io/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c16fe44c71af45e6b579ddf315237fbf"><span data-offset-key="c16fe44c71af45e6b579ddf315237fbf:0">https://www.pypa.io</span></span></a><span data-key="5ba51ba7570d40b6a489dd9540726b55"><span data-offset-key="5ba51ba7570d40b6a489dd9540726b55:0">, host projects on </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e422aa524acc4b89a74d5c5ba034ab59"><span data-offset-key="e422aa524acc4b89a74d5c5ba034ab59:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="49c72fa4cbb8492780afa4505c3eada3"><span data-offset-key="49c72fa4cbb8492780afa4505c3eada3:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://bitbucket.org/pypa" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2eabd4b585df454eaa70dd1ff6996f22"><span data-offset-key="2eabd4b585df454eaa70dd1ff6996f22:0">Bitbucket</span></span></a><span data-key="44c617ca829440fb845c33769b4c58c4"><span data-offset-key="44c617ca829440fb845c33769b4c58c4:0">, and discuss issues on the </span></span><a href="https://mail.python.org/mailman3/lists/distutils-sig.python.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="56715438979841da8c4cb2878299def2"><span data-offset-key="56715438979841da8c4cb2878299def2:0">distutils-sig mailing list</span></span></a><span data-key="81b785f9d46c4c2184244ec4461501d0"><span data-offset-key="81b785f9d46c4c2184244ec4461501d0:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://discuss.python.org/c/packaging" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fb27a441a9bc47c7b928a9c6fbd5498b"><span data-offset-key="fb27a441a9bc47c7b928a9c6fbd5498b:0">the Python Discourse forum</span></span></a><span data-key="fc1398825d744df3841ec41f3866c6c2"><span data-offset-key="fc1398825d744df3841ec41f3866c6c2:0">.Python Package Index (PyPI)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="fd665838f8f740bcad412989f90cbec3"><span data-offset-key="fd665838f8f740bcad412989f90cbec3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="665370b8da5041418e81fd2e44e5e44a"><span data-offset-key="665370b8da5041418e81fd2e44e5e44a:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="06b9fe33612c451bb032218be01723b5"><span data-offset-key="06b9fe33612c451bb032218be01723b5:0"> is the default </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Package-Index" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="803aeebcfd22431cbbd5e894bc85c3e1"><span data-offset-key="803aeebcfd22431cbbd5e894bc85c3e1:0">Package Index</span></span></a><span data-key="46e2db6e0c9c4c06814f34013c031cec"><span data-offset-key="46e2db6e0c9c4c06814f34013c031cec:0"> for the Python community. It is open to all Python developers to consume and distribute their distributions.pypi.org</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0cfedb65468d45a0904a167fbb6300c0"><span data-offset-key="0cfedb65468d45a0904a167fbb6300c0:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="441e3544d95e4099a802be4b9976436a"><span data-offset-key="441e3544d95e4099a802be4b9976436a:0">pypi.org</span></span></a><span data-key="69c0633e825c4569b52327f19b2c88cb"><span data-offset-key="69c0633e825c4569b52327f19b2c88cb:0"> is the domain name for the </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Python-Package-Index-PyPI" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7c2d2389131f4fd08c5c810e446d6bbb"><span data-offset-key="7c2d2389131f4fd08c5c810e446d6bbb:0">Python Package Index (PyPI)</span></span></a><span data-key="3ab0e17e96104d5dbd6f2a4b08097382"><span data-offset-key="3ab0e17e96104d5dbd6f2a4b08097382:0">. It replaced the legacy index domain name, </span><span data-offset-key="3ab0e17e96104d5dbd6f2a4b08097382:1">`pypi.python.org`</span><span data-offset-key="3ab0e17e96104d5dbd6f2a4b08097382:2">, in 2017. It is powered by </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#warehouse" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3cc28b7b9e404fed80397540d0f5a69e"><span data-offset-key="3cc28b7b9e404fed80397540d0f5a69e:0">Warehouse</span></span></a><span data-key="e402c41d49584f88965d47ea0cdb78a9"><span data-offset-key="e402c41d49584f88965d47ea0cdb78a9:0">.pyproject.toml</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="764d9c84f8c845c0b40142cdf26f3e16"><span data-offset-key="764d9c84f8c845c0b40142cdf26f3e16:0">The tool-agnostic </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Project" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ea7b89fabc86438c92472035996e2211"><span data-offset-key="ea7b89fabc86438c92472035996e2211:0">Project</span></span></a><span data-key="400133aa9d6c45999c816d45b66916b8"><span data-offset-key="400133aa9d6c45999c816d45b66916b8:0"> specification file. Defined in </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0518" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="24b289bf4e0548bb915dd8a428f7701b"><span data-offset-key="24b289bf4e0548bb915dd8a428f7701b:0"><strong>PEP 518</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="c0a920e1ff4b4eeda6fdd101ffcf5b19"><span data-offset-key="c0a920e1ff4b4eeda6fdd101ffcf5b19:0">.Release</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b58664a5ef4438e92a056ccc94f71ad"><span data-offset-key="1b58664a5ef4438e92a056ccc94f71ad:0">A snapshot of a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Project" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7be489adabc64efba670f0dbf02481f1"><span data-offset-key="7be489adabc64efba670f0dbf02481f1:0">Project</span></span></a><span data-key="a81785130f134dc5aec8e85df524d017"><span data-offset-key="a81785130f134dc5aec8e85df524d017:0"> at a particular point in time, denoted by a version identifier.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="73ed14aa050d433da1963095a1f10042"><span data-offset-key="73ed14aa050d433da1963095a1f10042:0">Making a release may entail the publishing of multiple </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6a11a7b9d0474282930b0cf76dbd37a2"><span data-offset-key="6a11a7b9d0474282930b0cf76dbd37a2:0">Distributions</span></span></a><span data-key="1c1e9cc06fad4b799e06149f0a3eac2f"><span data-offset-key="1c1e9cc06fad4b799e06149f0a3eac2f:0">. For example, if version 1.0 of a project was released, it could be available in both a source distribution format and a Windows installer distribution format.Requirement</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b772b73a18d4a3193a99e3a952b46d8"><span data-offset-key="1b772b73a18d4a3193a99e3a952b46d8:0">A specification for a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5c25c66702a14a0489fece5cf442824b"><span data-offset-key="5c25c66702a14a0489fece5cf442824b:0">package</span></span></a><span data-key="949fc28607be4534923d47132810178f"><span data-offset-key="949fc28607be4534923d47132810178f:0"> to be installed. </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bda675819ba24208ba742f3cdeab5ff3"><span data-offset-key="bda675819ba24208ba742f3cdeab5ff3:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="949bb6a144c343acbd55dda11120d6d6"><span data-offset-key="949bb6a144c343acbd55dda11120d6d6:0">, the </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Python-Packaging-Authority-PyPA" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a99ee819430e436f87434feb6bf2f6f9"><span data-offset-key="a99ee819430e436f87434feb6bf2f6f9:0">PYPA</span></span></a><span data-key="acb871800cb84b5aadc5da66653b97ac"><span data-offset-key="acb871800cb84b5aadc5da66653b97ac:0"> recommended installer, allows various forms of specification that can all be considered a “requirement”. For more information, see the </span></span><a href="https://pip.pypa.io/en/latest/cli/pip_install/#pip-install" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d595f5de2d704a2193055fd822016cfb"><span data-offset-key="d595f5de2d704a2193055fd822016cfb:0">pip install</span></span></a><span data-key="c0de69138b0e403bb6d8308d3c0ccf72"><span data-offset-key="c0de69138b0e403bb6d8308d3c0ccf72:0"> reference.Requirement Specifier</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9729f9e593b847249525460447ae743b"><span data-offset-key="9729f9e593b847249525460447ae743b:0">A format used by </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="95f7f66eaee442edb968672ca7cbf325"><span data-offset-key="95f7f66eaee442edb968672ca7cbf325:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="1b1f74de08ef408492e19dedbb290636"><span data-offset-key="1b1f74de08ef408492e19dedbb290636:0"> to install packages from a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Package-Index" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="03c398e0d8f6481295d35b1e973715d2"><span data-offset-key="03c398e0d8f6481295d35b1e973715d2:0">Package Index</span></span></a><span data-key="68689f9da0fb4b41b761c0507de657be"><span data-offset-key="68689f9da0fb4b41b761c0507de657be:0">. For an EBNF diagram of the format, see the </span></span><a href="https://setuptools.readthedocs.io/en/latest/pkg_resources.html#requirement-objects" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="efaba0a2ea4e4449a82906bc89d7e509"><span data-offset-key="efaba0a2ea4e4449a82906bc89d7e509:0">pkg_resources.Requirement</span></span></a><span data-key="36dfe0df4e124286b97d32ac31c78622"><span data-offset-key="36dfe0df4e124286b97d32ac31c78622:0"> entry in the </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="be3a7ba8349f4c858ca68f7fb61e41e9"><span data-offset-key="be3a7ba8349f4c858ca68f7fb61e41e9:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="c1113db8cb734aa2a318a7c8902eaa92"><span data-offset-key="c1113db8cb734aa2a318a7c8902eaa92:0"> docs. For example, “foo&gt;=1.3” is a requirement specifier, where “foo” is the project name, and the “&gt;=1.3” portion is the </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Version-Specifier" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="928805e938334b1aa167d716aa9cef2d"><span data-offset-key="928805e938334b1aa167d716aa9cef2d:0">Version Specifier</span></span></a><span data-key="d39b39b5a8714d688deadef13356fe6d"><span data-offset-key="d39b39b5a8714d688deadef13356fe6d:0">Requirements File</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e8208fe4d62649899b0b50f2ec38f12c"><span data-offset-key="e8208fe4d62649899b0b50f2ec38f12c:0">A file containing a list of </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Requirement" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c405f4058a9647508ceb2c2ddb653f16"><span data-offset-key="c405f4058a9647508ceb2c2ddb653f16:0">Requirements</span></span></a><span data-key="61a12e9baf8447e1ad12ffb17527f02c"><span data-offset-key="61a12e9baf8447e1ad12ffb17527f02c:0"> that can be installed using </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="11a67a94a2ba484ab2df007299cb6634"><span data-offset-key="11a67a94a2ba484ab2df007299cb6634:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="05fa8b40a83d4773973744275e8bde2d"><span data-offset-key="05fa8b40a83d4773973744275e8bde2d:0">. For more information, see the </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3bfe9e87ae4543db879d3cfadeb998ce"><span data-offset-key="3bfe9e87ae4543db879d3cfadeb998ce:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="0753865fd33646338637e79fe73a8bfa"><span data-offset-key="0753865fd33646338637e79fe73a8bfa:0"> docs on </span></span><a href="https://pip.pypa.io/en/latest/user_guide/#requirements-files" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fd01666325e74862ac666e5bbb47237e"><span data-offset-key="fd01666325e74862ac666e5bbb47237e:0">Requirements Files</span></span></a><span data-key="b20ac8bdb1f440ea9e7f12f3acc81904"><span data-offset-key="b20ac8bdb1f440ea9e7f12f3acc81904:0">.setup.pysetup.cfg</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ae5eb4e7a6b947bb812a7f898884b030"><span data-offset-key="ae5eb4e7a6b947bb812a7f898884b030:0">The project specification files for </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#distutils" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b0fdabbe04cd429a83e189d93fb49e99"><span data-offset-key="b0fdabbe04cd429a83e189d93fb49e99:0">distutils</span></span></a><span data-key="3e8d8703585047acbd3c4315bcafdf56"><span data-offset-key="3e8d8703585047acbd3c4315bcafdf56:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3ab2b67bd6a2417c8d060524280a6f88"><span data-offset-key="3ab2b67bd6a2417c8d060524280a6f88:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="20661a94e8614b25afa6ca89b198e542"><span data-offset-key="20661a94e8614b25afa6ca89b198e542:0">. See also </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-pyproject.toml" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c4f7e2fc72e34c5083aced2b1327bdf2"><span data-offset-key="c4f7e2fc72e34c5083aced2b1327bdf2:0">pyproject.toml</span></span></a><span data-key="9a43ccfbc45d4973ba5cdeaeba3ac43e"><span data-offset-key="9a43ccfbc45d4973ba5cdeaeba3ac43e:0">.Source Archive</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2c368eb2cf194785b1066cdc8ec08452"><span data-offset-key="2c368eb2cf194785b1066cdc8ec08452:0">An archive containing the raw source code for a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Release" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2cfc686823e84d93a60d9d30926b9c27"><span data-offset-key="2cfc686823e84d93a60d9d30926b9c27:0">Release</span></span></a><span data-key="420dbc4d43dc45d7aabbe79c1d6e321e"><span data-offset-key="420dbc4d43dc45d7aabbe79c1d6e321e:0">, prior to creation of a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Source-Distribution-or-sdist" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="52636589d55a4a958b9740312920513b"><span data-offset-key="52636589d55a4a958b9740312920513b:0">Source Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="2cf9876c92fe403b92e4d1090dc723e7"><span data-offset-key="2cf9876c92fe403b92e4d1090dc723e7:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Built-Distribution" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b5f2f01ec09248adba169115bf330574"><span data-offset-key="b5f2f01ec09248adba169115bf330574:0">Built Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="d9c839ab1c2e4a36b2aa38fa7c459e4e"><span data-offset-key="d9c839ab1c2e4a36b2aa38fa7c459e4e:0">.Source Distribution (or “sdist”)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1d54ff46e3a24c868c9b4b97f4f3d66c"><span data-offset-key="1d54ff46e3a24c868c9b4b97f4f3d66c:0">A </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dd9a27cee2d6446ab0e2bd16b7e7e261"><span data-offset-key="dd9a27cee2d6446ab0e2bd16b7e7e261:0">distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="7d825d26f8944e09ab1e7a266f4f6270"><span data-offset-key="7d825d26f8944e09ab1e7a266f4f6270:0"> format (usually generated using </span><span data-offset-key="7d825d26f8944e09ab1e7a266f4f6270:1">`python setup.py sdist`</span><span data-offset-key="7d825d26f8944e09ab1e7a266f4f6270:2">) that provides metadata and the essential source files needed for installing by a tool like </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2ed08fdd39ad4dc7b739250b894c28f6"><span data-offset-key="2ed08fdd39ad4dc7b739250b894c28f6:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="841607ba7797479dbb6d47e219a36535"><span data-offset-key="841607ba7797479dbb6d47e219a36535:0">, or for generating a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Built-Distribution" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a421937bc1184e8cb8a7fbec1b169b6d"><span data-offset-key="a421937bc1184e8cb8a7fbec1b169b6d:0">Built Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="b592f04d2cbd40e2976571a3878d251d"><span data-offset-key="b592f04d2cbd40e2976571a3878d251d:0">.System Package</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7f0e1a45c3214d45bc451121d3f03001"><span data-offset-key="7f0e1a45c3214d45bc451121d3f03001:0">A package provided in a format native to the operating system, e.g. an rpm or dpkg file.Version Specifier</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9d4267026e9847a6890ac05b0f30769e"><span data-offset-key="9d4267026e9847a6890ac05b0f30769e:0">The version component of a </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Requirement-Specifier" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d169635d67904777969b0adf400bc523"><span data-offset-key="d169635d67904777969b0adf400bc523:0">Requirement Specifier</span></span></a><span data-key="2c984d91895c45ab9d88971f3a1c4007"><span data-offset-key="2c984d91895c45ab9d88971f3a1c4007:0">. For example, the “&gt;=1.3” portion of “foo&gt;=1.3”. </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0440" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="dc4f5f1a2ed94e3282e0a07624e32782"><span data-offset-key="dc4f5f1a2ed94e3282e0a07624e32782:0"><strong>PEP 440</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="dc32ce45e4fc45e6b5a1a3316d54c18b"><span data-offset-key="dc32ce45e4fc45e6b5a1a3316d54c18b:0"> contains a </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0440#version-specifiers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5d06c864417a4b7f86c253b89a56edc0"><span data-offset-key="5d06c864417a4b7f86c253b89a56edc0:0"><strong>full specification</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="cd914905fdcb43e7bac31364b01236e0"><span data-offset-key="cd914905fdcb43e7bac31364b01236e0:0"> of the specifiers that Python packaging currently supports. Support for PEP440 was implemented in </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e87ef8567331440bbc67c341d6868935"><span data-offset-key="e87ef8567331440bbc67c341d6868935:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="94f2208a1c6b4fd4a108fe5d84aa2242"><span data-offset-key="94f2208a1c6b4fd4a108fe5d84aa2242:0"> v8.0 and </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7efac9fd768445e787ca27edabca6a23"><span data-offset-key="7efac9fd768445e787ca27edabca6a23:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="a03ef3e8009549128911391171bff46a"><span data-offset-key="a03ef3e8009549128911391171bff46a:0"> v6.0.Virtual Environment</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Virtual-Environment" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1967cf1a05774e1d9ba00d1afdbb3c29"><span data-offset-key="1967cf1a05774e1d9ba00d1afdbb3c29:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="dfccd794e1ea47cfbda9cb584b50da8e"><span data-offset-key="dfccd794e1ea47cfbda9cb584b50da8e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e48e42dd854d4942963e3a5b0eab8b60"><span data-offset-key="e48e42dd854d4942963e3a5b0eab8b60:0">An isolated Python environment that allows packages to be installed for use by a particular application, rather than being installed system wide. For more information, see the section on </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/tutorials/installing-packages/#creating-and-using-virtual-environments" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="16319a938e3147d9b9fccf7d07098e59"><span data-offset-key="16319a938e3147d9b9fccf7d07098e59:0">Creating Virtual Environments</span></span></a><span data-key="0e7a925bae954bca894f31155d1e1945"><span data-offset-key="0e7a925bae954bca894f31155d1e1945:0">.Wheel</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="66b94470858643a887b65d6255252be6"><span data-offset-key="66b94470858643a887b65d6255252be6:0">A </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Built-Distribution" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="57f1ef66c65e4e248812de4174c805b7"><span data-offset-key="57f1ef66c65e4e248812de4174c805b7:0">Built Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="8762bb18e9c248f08ec80a7621dfc66a"><span data-offset-key="8762bb18e9c248f08ec80a7621dfc66a:0"> format introduced by </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0427" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6446175230d2442d941940726c99669b"><span data-offset-key="6446175230d2442d941940726c99669b:0"><strong>PEP 427</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="f80e6fccd3444a64932bdac6b78d415c"><span data-offset-key="f80e6fccd3444a64932bdac6b78d415c:0">, which is intended to replace the </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Egg" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0df679894ad548f1bdb2630dec62d271"><span data-offset-key="0df679894ad548f1bdb2630dec62d271:0">Egg</span></span></a><span data-key="b391720dcc9c456eb221aa4f38956c11"><span data-offset-key="b391720dcc9c456eb221aa4f38956c11:0"> format. Wheel is currently supported by </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="456cbbfc80844d22861ab78d359f7d0a"><span data-offset-key="456cbbfc80844d22861ab78d359f7d0a:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="1996047dc24c49a8818c2e2857927b17"><span data-offset-key="1996047dc24c49a8818c2e2857927b17:0">.Working Set</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a9962b84af9349dcb36630d5c8b0014b"><span data-offset-key="a9962b84af9349dcb36630d5c8b0014b:0">A collection of </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="db8fe2d651c848019384a703c475373c"><span data-offset-key="db8fe2d651c848019384a703c475373c:0">distributions</span></span></a><span data-key="d01a6a3748d0440ca3a5aa0d06214d44"><span data-offset-key="d01a6a3748d0440ca3a5aa0d06214d44:0"> available for importing. These are the distributions that are on the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/sys.html#sys.path" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5dd03f950abf4434accc50e9d6635bd5"><span data-offset-key="5dd03f950abf4434accc50e9d6635bd5:0"><code class="code-0458e21e" spellcheck="false" data-slate-leaf="true">sys.path</code></span></span></a><span data-key="17bc93ba98a34f72a7d940980a58d62a"><span data-offset-key="17bc93ba98a34f72a7d940980a58d62a:0"> variable. At most, one </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ce5b9064a3b54259ac07e4a55c693ea4"><span data-offset-key="ce5b9064a3b54259ac07e4a55c693ea4:0">Distribution</span></span></a><span data-key="fdd5551bc95c4269a6c228f3f4d33e0f"><span data-offset-key="fdd5551bc95c4269a6c228f3f4d33e0f:0"> for a project is possible in a working set.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--UIH300-2063425d--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span class="text-4505230f--UIH200-50ead35f--textContentFamily-49a318e1">Glossary</span></span>
